# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Tewwet ad tɛeǧǧer, ad tessers afus-is ɣef wammas is, twala tuli-tt tassemt almi ula d lqedd-is ur yebḍa ara. Tneqqel abruɛ i tqendurt-is, tufa tiqesbuḍin-is tweccem-itent tudert. Ttbanen-d fell-asent iṣerdan ǧǧan wussan.

# Tewwi-d acewwiq :

Asmi i d-yusa zzehr-iw,

Nekk yufa-yi-d di tebḥirt

Lxalat megrent irden,

Nekk la meggreɣ tamezzirt

A yessetma wagi d…

Ass-a iṭij yesskew aglim-is, yeqqur yuɣal am ulemsir.

Amzur-is yenncew, tɣumm-it s thendit. Uraden icettiḍen, truḥ ad ten-tefser di tebḥirt. Tṣubb lekmam-is ammar ad yili win ara tt-id-iwalin. Tejbed taqendurt-is akken ur tneṭṭed ara ɣef weksum-is, akken ad teṣṣer leɛyub-is. Tiɣilt terɣa. Tessaked akka n wakka, ulac yiwen, ala ajrad iɛemmren iḥerqan.

# Tewwi-d acewwiq :

Asmi i d-yusa zzehr-iw,

Nekk yufa-yi-d di lexla…

Ass-a tessen d acu i d layas. Tessen d acu i d lmut, ɣas acḥal aya segmi teẓra belli temmut. Acḥal aya segmi i tt-teṭṭafar am tili-ines. Tessarem ad s-terwel... Teɛreḍ ad d-tekk nnig-s. Ur s-tezmir ara. Ass-a tebra i ṭṭbel deg waman, teǧǧa-as ad tt-tali am tara…

Texza cciṭan…

Ṣṣut iruḥ-d seg umeẓẓuɣ-is :

- A Fa... bedd-asen-d i warrac ad ččen imekli d lawan...
- A Fa…
- A F…

Simi i d-yewweḍ yiḍ teɣli, tekfa tezmert n temẓi. Tefka idis-is i lqaɛa… A tettfay, teẓẓel afus-is, ulac d acu ara tt-id-iḥazen, weltma-s tezweǧ. Ḥala lweḥc i d-yeggran, yezzi-as si yal tama.

Tiɣmert n wexxam d tilemt… Dayen tura, tuɣ tannumi yid-s. Temdel allen-is. Tessemḥes i tfekka-s ammar ad d-tsuɣ... Ǧǧan-tt isuɣan. Tnuda ammar ad sen-tsel i yiqjan i ihebbren deg-s deg yiḍ. Ad tɣilleḍ nnejmaɛen. Ḥala lḥekkat-is akked weɛrur-is i la ihebbren deg-s seg weqraḥ.

- Yekfa ssuq tenza sselɛa…

# Tacmat

# Said CHEMAKH

1. Yeffe$ wawal, taddart akk tesla s wehdum. Ahdum d Caâban Cterriê i t-ixedmen, isem-is s tuffra i t-id-qarren medden armi yu$al mi t-id-tbedrev am akken d aîeyyeê i d-tîeyyêev ! Cterriê yekker-d di taddart am netta am medden $as akken baba-s maççi di taddart i d-ilul. Yusa-d di 1920, yedduri leânaya n At Lêusin.

Baba-s irwel si Temguî $ef temgarî yen$a. At Lêusin fkan-as akal, rnan zewoen-as, yeooa-d yiwen weqcic : d Cterriê Caâban. Ula d Beééi seg At Lêusin i d-yezweo : yu$ yiwet n tmeîîut d zzin, isem-is Mekyusa.

Mi yemmut baba-s, Caâban ibedd $ef yemma-s, akken iqwem ur txuû deg wacemma. Isâa taqcict akked weqcic. Taqcict isemma-yas Nila, $er yemma-s Mekyusa i tettemcabi di zzin, di lqedd, di vrafa... di kkulec. Nila tetturebba akken ilaq, am tullas n taddart. Mi tebbev 16 iseggasen, tettban-d d tameîîut, lad$a bdant tnexvabin ad d-kkatent $er Mekyusa : yal ta teb$a-tt i mmi-s ! Nila, ur d-telha ara d temsal-agi n tissulya ne$ lexvubegga. I tt-ice$ben êala leqraya-s. Attan d$a agguren ineggura ur d-teclig deg wacemma siwa aheggi n lbak ara tesâeddi di yunyu.

Caâban ifreê aîas s yelli-s : tessen ad t$er, tqeddec deg wexxam, yerna tecbeê terêa akk ulawen n yilmeéyen n taddart wamma arrac ukud teqqar, ur d-neqqar.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 91 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Yiwen ur yeéri amek i bdant tirga tisseîîafin tta$ent deg wul n Caâban. Acêal aya turan, ur d-ikeççem ara s axxam alamma yewwet-itt-d d ssekran ula d abrid ur t-yettaâqal. Akken, akken... zi$ yir tikta $ef yelli-s frurint deg walla$-is. Yeqqel yedderwec fell-as akter n yilmeéyen-nni yeb$an Nila. Si âemrayen-nni ideg yekcem, xerbent-as akk. D$a yerra-tt i lweâd n tissit. Ar taggara yerwi at wexxam, yerwi akk medden. Maççi d abrid i txeîîan di tejmaât $ef rregmat, $ef usexûer... ad d-yekker tifawt acemma ur yelli : ma tenniv-as ma telha tin txedmev ivelli ne$ mdeh, tebra ma yeéra, ma yecfa. Ad yeffe$ $er zdat wexxam ad iqqim din ad yessikid di yelli-s amek tqeddec, ne$ teqqar... Tura, yir tikta-nni bdant la d-gemmunt. Ïarent-as, d$a ad iûubb $er lbar n Zizi Äebdella, ad d-isker.

Mekyusa sked akken ur teâriv ad as-teddu di leb$i i wergaz-is. Ulac, mi tenîeq $er-s ad tt-id-yeçç s rregmat, ma yewâa-tt atan ad teçç ti$rit. Ma d Nila, yesmeêsis-as mi ara s-d-tettmeslay, mi ara s-tessers imekli ne$ imensi. Allen-is ur tekksent ara si tedmarin n teqcic, si tqemmuct-is, seg wemzur-is ne$ seg wammas-is.

Yeshetrif di lbar armi t-id-ssuf$en warrac n taddart akken qrib yennu$ akked kra isekranen i t-yecban. Iteddu yeshetrif... Acu-t akka i la d-yeqqar mi akken yeswa ? Atan wacu i wumi d-cfan ileméiyen-nni n taddart :

- ... Teb$am-tt, ééi$-tt, neqce$-tt, tura dayen tessenîi, teb$am-tt ! Tebra yiwen ur tt-yeççi, imi nekk âettbe$ fell-as kunwi tusam-d ad tt-teççem s tevsa, d nekk ara tt-yeççen... Tessenîi d nekk ara iâerven tasenîit-is...

Arrac ur fhimen tigert : $ilen d acu n tneqlet-agi âzizen fell-as i wuççi am t$animt, d zzit-lxadem ne$ d kra n tcetwit... i$ef yugad ad as-xerrfen medden... A zi$ netta d yelli-s Nila i icebba $er tneqlet ! Maca di tallit yiwen yerra ddhen-is $er yir ssuq ideg yebberttax Caâban. Nwan akk medden ha zi$ netta ihav.

£ilen medden itess akken ad yekkes urfan, zi$ netta ibâed s anda i yessuref di tirga, d ayen ur itekkes ccrab i$ef yerza...

Di bujember, yebda llqev n uzemmur, arrac n lakul ttawin-d 15 wussan n westaâfu n tegrest. Akken ula d Nila,

- 92 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

issaê-itt-id westaâfu, tenwa ad têaref deg wussan-nni ad tessen$es kra di t$uri i tt-yeggunin ssya $er lbak. Yuli wass, Nila ur tedda ara $er llqev uzemmur. Tteklen fell-as at wexxam ad asen-d-tesseww imekli, ad asen-t-tceggaâ i win ara yadren $er Tniri. Telha-d d leqdic : tessirid, tesserkam, tessehmay-d, tesseww-d a$rum... Tikkelt-nni, atan yekcem-d baba-s. Akken i t-twala tezmumeg-as d tavsa, tenna-yas :

- Lâeslama a baba ! Imekli qrib ad yewjed...

Yevsa-yas, yenna-yas ad as-tawi lqehwa $er uûalu. Nila s t$awalt i terra takaftirt $ef tkuzint akken ad as-d-theggi i baba-s lqehwa. Di snat ddqayeq, yers-d ufenoal, ssker, tavebsit n te$rifin... $ef ssniwa. Akken d-tuli lqehwa, tessmar-itt $er t$ellayt. Tewwi-yas-tt i baba-s.

Akken tt-tessers $ef îîabla yeîîef-itt-id seg ufus yenna-yas :

- Qim tura a yelli ad teswev ciî yid-i, acêal aya ur nqesser ara akken...

Tenna-yas Nila :

- Yerbeê a baba, rou kan ad ssexsi$ i ufurnu ne$ mulac ad yer$ usseqi...

Teqqim $er tama n baba-s.

# 2.

Afus n baba-s yennev-d i tuyat-is ; tecmumeê-as : t$il tme$bunt d leêmala i tt-iêemmel baba-s, icedha-tt, yeb$a ad as-yesbin leênana-s... Di ddeqs-zzalla, tufa-d iman-is teééel $ef ukanapi, taqendurt tuli, baba-s yu$al fell-as... Ur d-tecfa i wacemma êala mi têulfa i tâeddist-is tegzem, tcerreg, idim seg-s yettfeggiv... Tsu$ :

- Ayy ! Anna$ a baba...

Ur d-tfukk awal, yerra-yas afus-is $ef yimi... Tserreê d imeîîi acku teéra ass-nni i tfukk tiéeî di tmeddurt-is...

Caâban am yilef : la ilehhet amzun d tirkeft n wuccayen i tt-id-yeddan fell-as. Mi t-id-ccfent tidiwin n tecmat, yezzi $er yelli-s, idemmer-itt te$li seg ukanapi-nni, yenna-yas :

- Ffe$ ur kem-ttwali$ ara a l... a yelli-s n leê..., digaj a taqjunt...

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 93 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Taqcict teffe$-d seg wexxam s tazzla. Imeîîawen ttmiren-d seg wallen-is, idammen mazal urâad qquren $ef tqendurt-is d yivarren-is. Sekkura d tajaret-nsen i tt-id-iwalan d tamezwarut mi d-tehmel deg wezniq n taddart, tezzazzel $er-s, temme$ fell-as teîîef-itt-id seg ufus tenna-yas :

- D acu a yelli ? D acu yevran ?…
- D baba…

Tajaret-nni n wexxam n Cterriê akken twala idammen mazal ttmirin-d $ef ivarren n teqcict tsu$, tenna :

- Abbuh ay at leârav !… Dayen ifukk leqder di taddart-a, d lâar i yu$en amkan-is…

Xelluoa n Ëmed, d tameîîut tamezwarut i s-d-yeslan seg ucario anda i tu$ la tettacar tibettit n waman, tuzzel-d, tenna-yasent :

- D acu ? d acu yevran ?…

Ayen deg tmuqel di Sekkura, tefhem asigna i s-tekkat, tenna-yas :

- D anwa akka i s-ixedmen i teqcict-a akka ?…

Nila tettru kan, ma d Sekkura tenna-yas :

- D anwa i t$ilev ad s-yexdem akka ? d baba-s…

Ixeddamen ucanîi yellan qqazen tasilya $ef yiri n webrid n taddart akken sersen iqudas n waman slan-d i têaêayt yekkren, ulin-d ula d nutni maca mi d-wwven $er wezniq ur ten-walant ara tlawin, yerna slan-d i yalci mmeslayent. Akken faqent wwven-d yirgazen, tenîeq Xelluoa tenna-yasent i Sekkura d teqcict-nni tame$bunt :

- Lêumt s axxam-iw maççi dagi a neqqim…

Tilawin ddant akken d tarbaât s axxam n Xelluoa. Llant snat ne$ tlata n tiyav i d-yewwven mbaâd. Ma d ixeddamen ucanîi fehmen akk tamsalt maca yiwen ur d-yenni awal. Mi wwven $er tsilya-nni la tt$izin, yenîeq yiwen $er wayev yenna-yas :

- D$a d wagi tura i d argaz ? Yewwi-d ad yemmzel deffir temgerî…
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Yenîeq-d yiwen seg yimeddukal-is yenna:

- Wah ! ula d keçç, zi$ la tesheôwivev !… Anwa ara yezlun aqjun am winna ? Ad $anfun medden ula d tinilit ad t-nnalen…
- Ihi ad as-tanfev kan ad yesserwat ; ma yekkes sser $ef yelli-s, yekkes-it $ef wexxam-is, $ef twacult-is, $ef taddart-nne$ i merra. Maççi d ayen ara neqbel ?
- Qbel ne$ qim, ulay txedmev ! Asmi i yeffe$ tajmiât i neéra belli ur yelli kra ara d-yasen n wayen yelhan si tama-s… Asmi i d-yenna iqerray bvan, ixxamen bvan i nebna ad nawev $er tegnit am ta…
- Ur as-nettanfet ara ad yesserwat akken yeb$a êala aya ur nqebbel ara ?

Yenna-yas yiwen nniven:

- Ur t-tessinev ara ; ur yeffi$ ara leânaya n At Lêusin armi yedduri tin n ioadarmiyen. D netta i d landikatur-nsen di taddart-a ! Wamag amek ara éren belli Kamal u Ëennuc d akuminist ? Amek ara éren belli arrac-nni n Ti$ilt xeddmen akked werbeâ-nni n Imazi$en ? D Caâban i sen-yettawin akk tixbirin n taddart. Limer ad t-tennalem ad d-yawev Brigadyi tameddit-a ad yexdem axeûûar deg-wen...
- Saêêa a zzman ideg i d-neggra ! Lbaîel âinani yerna ur tezmirev ad k-id-yali wawal !...
- Über ! ad d-yawev wass ad ifakk...

# Karim At Zeyyan d aqcic si tddart d-iqerben $er At Knuda.

Yella yeqqar di llisi akked Nila. Iêemmel-itt aîas, yeêseb-itt am mummu n tiî-is ne$ ugar. Asmi yu$al $er llisi, yufan Nila ur d-tu$al ara. Yekker yesteqsa, ulac win i s-d-yefkan isallen fell-as, ulac win ne$ tin i tt-yeéran segmi teffe$ di dujambar si llisi. Inuda-d $er taddart, yesteqsa, yufa-d yakan kra n yilmeéyen yesteqsa-ten. Mi éran anwa-t, ur s-nnin ara tidet s lekmal ; nnan-as kan yeêbes-itt-id baba-s $ef t$uri. Inuda ad iéer baba-s n Nila. Mmlan-as-t ; di lbar n Si Äebdella i yeddewwir. Iruê $er-s.

# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Mbaâd sslam, yenna-yas Caâban :

- Acu-t akka i k-id-yecqan a mmi ?...
- Usi$-d ad steqsi$ $ef Nila...
- D acu-yak-tt akken ad testeqsiv fell-as ?
- Neqqar akken di llisi...
- Ihi dayen tfukk t$uri, ifukk llisi...

Aqcic iêar acu ara d-yini. Yeb$a ad as-yini “acu$er ?”, “Ayen?”... maca awal inneqmav, tiyersi tcudd.

Yeârev yenna-yas :

- Acu d ssebba ,

Yenna-yas Caâban :

- Axaîer isab llxux i wefrux ! ha ! ha !...

Yerna wayen yerna, Karim yuzen-d imawlan-is axxam n Nila, qesden-d i nnesba. Wid d-yusan ur ssinen ara taddart. Mi steqsan $ef wexxam n Caâban Cterriê, îîfen-ten at-taddart nnan-asen tidet yeffren. U$alen mebla ma wwven s axxam n teqcict. Karim yerfa $ef yimawlan-is mi s nnan :

- Ur ak-d-nxeîîeb ara yir taqcict...

Yekker inuda, yesteqsa armi d-yiwi tidet amek tella. Maca yugi ad yebru i taluft, yegguma ad yamen. Ize$deddi kan di yiwet n takti, yettkezziz kan deg-s : ilaq ad ya$ Nila i yeb$un yili.

Mi slan akk medden s tcemat iga Caâban Cterriê di taddart n At Knuda, kkren kra n warrac n wedrum n Karim îîfen-t nnan-as :

- I tura keçç s leâqel-ik i telliv, mi akka tessaliv tasawent i yimawlan-ik ? Ad ak-qqaren taqcict tesâa lâib wamma atan wwin-ak-tt-id. Teb$iv ad ak-t-id-yekfu baba-k s yir imeslayen.

èran akk medden belli Nila-agi i$ef $-teççiv aqerru icerrem-itt baba-s. S tefransist d l’inceste... Dayen, maççi d tanubit. Anwa ara k-ya$en tin ur yellin d tanubit ? Abeâda ma d baba-s i tt-ifellqen ?…

Zzin-as armi yebra i wawal, armi yenfa isem n Nila seg yimi-s. £as tella tayri maca tezwar tmetti, tezwar wayen i wumi qqaren di kra n tudrin "lêerma". Karim yerra timedlin i wul :

maççi d netta ur yeb$in ara Nila $as maççi d tanubit, $as d baba-s i tt-yeccemten... d at twacult-is, d at taddart-is, d timetti s umata.

- 96 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Nila yemmut zzher-is; mi d-usan inexvaben, ad qqlen si taddart mebla ma wwven-d s axxam. Akken kan ara slen s wehdum yessker baba-s ad ddzen abrid n tu$alin. Anwa i ara iqeblen ad yawi i mmi-s taqcict ur nelli d tanubit? Yerna nnig waya d baba-s i tt-yeccemten... Yerna éran akk medden... Ulac...

Nnan wid yuran tizmamin $ef tmetti taqbaylit belli Leqbayel ulac win iteggen azal i nnif d lêerma am nitni. Ahat d tidet yella waya. Maca tella kra n tidet ilaq ad tt-id-nini: ulac tirect ur nesâi akerfa. Ma yella win d-yekkren ad ak-yini d nekni, nettgalla s "jmeâliman"... Atan ihi tûubb s anda ur d-tettali. Acku, gar ciî d waîas, ilaq ad nâiwed tamu$li di tmetti, ad nessiwev ad d-nini yiwet n tidet: tameîîut tettwaêqer, ur tesâi kra d azref... Iêqa, tesâa azref ad tru $ef zzher-is ne$ sseâd-is.

Wid yerran tameîîut d nnif d lêerma, zeglen yiwet, ccven. Akken i k-yenna yiwen umaru: ur tufiv anda ara sersen nnif-nsen alamma gar ivarren n tmeîîut! Ufan tamkant, yerna d tin igerrzen, ad tt-iêrez Rebbi!

Tinnubya n teqcict d aswir âlayen akk di lêerma $er Leqbayel. Acêal d tin d-yebran êala $ef waya: ur telli ara d tanubit! Acêal d tin yezla baba-s ne$ gma-s $ef waya. D tidet, timetti tettbeddil, maca yella waya. Tinnubya n teqcict teqqel d tawtilt segmi d-yella unbav n ubabat $ef tmetti (patriarcat), wamma asmi yella wenbav n tmeîîut (matriarcat), ulac kra din.

Imawlan lad$a tilawin ttêarabent êala $ef tinnubya n yessi-tsent am terwiêt-nsent. Ur ilaq ara ad awvent s ixxamen n yirgazen mebla tinnubya acku d lâib: "taqcict ara yaf wergaz teldi ad tt-id-yerr di sebâa wussan!" i qqarent tlawin. Teqqel akka i d lâadda am kra n leâwayed ur nemâin ideg i skabecren kra. Acku anwa i inudan argaz ma d anubi? £ef tmeîîut kan yezgan di taddart i d-yewwi waya? Irgazen maâlic ma xerrqen deg iburdilen ne$ deg kra n yexxamen di temdinin? Deg waya txuûû te$demt. Txuûû aîas...

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 97 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Si zzman n zik, ttasen-d waâraben $er taddart n Tgemmunt. Ttasen-d zaooawen irden, timéin… Ttaoowen ini$man, zzit… Ahat si qbel ddewla n Fransa i tella lâadda-agi n tisin-nsen $er tmurt n Leqbayel. Mbaâd u$alen kra n waâraben, ttasen-d akken ad xedmen : llan wid yettruéun aéru deg yiberdan la txeddem ddewla i wumi qqaren Lehoares, llan kra ssifin u ttâemmiren ajdi deg yisaffen, wiyav xeddmen deg yicanîiyen n lebni… Yal yiwen amek. Mi tâedda taluft n Tefsut n 80, aîas i yegguman ad d-u$alen $er tmurt n Leqbayel acku di tallit-nni llant temnavin anda i sen-sser$en medden iâecciwen-nsen. Maca ddewla tazzayrit terra-d aîas deg-sen : mi sen-thudd iâecciwen anda nniven ad asen-d-fken lekwa$ev ad d-asen $er tmurt n Leqbayel. Mi d-wwven, ddewla ad asen-tefk ixxamen, axeddim… Di tallit-nni qqaren-as i tsertit-agi s tefransist : "des populations", s taârabt "imdizao assukani". Tedda akka tallit armi d aseggas-nni n 1988. D$a yalci ibeddel. Maca mazal aâraben ttasen-d zznuzen abiûar, timéin, akraren, i$yal… di leswaq n temdinin tikwal, ttalin ula $er tuddar.

Di tallit-nni, yusa-d yiwen waârab la yezznuz i$yal, isem-is Qwider. Ur iban amek i d-ijuba tamusni akked Cterriê. Nadi tura amek i ttemyussanen yimdanen ne$ amek ttemsefhamen $ef aya d wayen. Ihi, Cterriê yefka-yas yelli-s i Qwider-nni ; meêsub s nnesba n Lislam ; awi-d ccix ara ye$ren lfattiêa zdat inagan, zzwao qqaren "zdat Rebbi d lâibad-is" ! Ah ya ddin uqabac mi ara twaliv nnesba amek i tettili $ur leonas nniven, ad tmemmiv ad teççev abaskiv yumsen aluv ! Ih ! Ne$ ahat d rruda n wetraktur !

Cterriê yerna yefka-yas i uveggal-is taxxamt anda yezde$ netta d yelli-s. D taxxamt i yeîîurften $ef taddart. Qwider yemmut si lfeôê ; netta i yellan d amzenzi n ye$yal, yu$ taqbaylit… Yemme$ yefka-yas yiwen we$yul d ayen i d netta i Cterriê, u yenna-yas :

- Atan wagi d lehdeyya stadir d tarzeft s$ur-i !

# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Yebda Qwider la yettxemmim amek a yeldi lkumirs di taddart akken ad d-yettawi sselâa si Sidi Äisa, ad tt-yeznuz di Tgemmunt u amek ara yettaoew zzit d ini$man ad ten-yettawi ad ten-yezzenz anda nniven. Yenna-yas i uveggal-is ma yeqbel ad ccerken akken. Cterriê yeqbel.

At taddart, yiwen deg-s ur d-yeclig deg wayen d-yellan gar Qwider d Cterriê. Di tazwara, llan wid i$av lêal $ef teqcict acku $ur-sen tuklal argaz imeânen maççi am uzenzi n ye$yal; llan wiyav la s-qqaren si leûlaê imi d-tufa win i tt-yu$en acku s tecmat i s-d-yevran ulac win ara iqeblen ad tt-ya$. Llan da$en wid ur ikerhen aâraben, ur ten-yeâoib ara lêal akken llan di$en wid i sen-yennan imi ur teb$im ara ad tt-ya$ waârab, acu$er ulac ula yiwen deg-wen i tt-ixevben… Lêaûul At Tgemmunt sâan akk rray, yal wa amek i t-id-yenna…

Tâedda tallit, yalwa yelha-d d wayen i t-ice$ben. Yiwen wass yennu$ Qwider akked Cterriê $ef yidrimen. Mserwin yiwen ur yefhim amek. Yusa-d Qwider $er tejmiât n taddart yenna-yas :

- Ay at taddart, imi taswiât akka i tiwev, init-as i Cterriê-agi-nwen ad iyi-d-yerr a$yul-iw, ne$ nekk atan si tura ad as-d-rre$ yelli-s…
- Äeddit tura frut-tent ay at ttwab! Yekker herwel di taddart; $ilen hennan si Cterriê d tecmatin-is, zi$en simmal mazal la ten-yerêu… Kkren-d kra n yilmeéyen nnan-as :
- Ad t-nawi s asif, ad nefru tamsalt-is i lebda.
- Maca kkren kra n yim$aren, seg wid yezzuzufen lêif nnan-as :
- Ur t-tneqqem ara aydi, aneft-as ad yemmurves alamma la yessutur lmut nettat ad tagi ad d-tas…

Zzin $er Qwider fran-tt yid-s u nnan-as :

- Tamsalt-agi n yidrimen yella wamek ara tt-nefru. A$yul-ik ad t-tawiv maca acrak yid-s ifukk. Ma d tameîîut d tameîîut-ik yiwen ur yezmir ad k-tt-yekkes $as i lukan d baba-s…

Rnan mmeslayen d Qwider acêal. Mi d-ye$li yiv, usan-d kra n yirgazen n Tgemmunt $er texxamt-nni ideg yezde$ Qwider. Ufan-t-id iâebba kra d sselâa yesâa s akamyun.

# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

terkeb tama-s $er zdat. Mi ten-iwala wwven nehôen-d a$yul-nni, yers-d seg ukamyun, yenna-yasen :

- Di laânaya-nwen ma ur iyi-tsemiêem, aîas i ken-êeîîne$ !

Maca a$yul-agi, ûeddqe$-t i taddart, fket-t i walbaâv ime$ban ad yexdem yis-s laé-is. Taqcict-nwen d zzwao i zewoe$ yid-s, maççi d abeddel i tt-beddle$ s we$yul… Qimet di lehna, ad ken-iâin Rebbi di cc$el-nwen…

Ma d Nila, d awez$i tezzi-d $er Tgemmunt : ula asmi yemmut baba-s…

# Aseklu n temẓi

Mourad ZIMU

Di taddart-iw aseklu,

Seddaw-as akk i nett$imi,

Di ccetwa ne$ deg unebdu

Nettdaray, yerra tili,

Issel akk ayen i nêekku,

D anagi iceffu,

Nessawal-as aseklu n teméi.

A sidi u lbaba-inu, amzun di tmucuha, aseklu-agi nêemmel-it akk, yezga-d $ef yiri n webrid, zzint-as teblavin, nett$ima fell-asent, wa yetturar tiddas, wa iêekku tixidas.

Lêaûun, aseklu i$ef ara d-neêku, yu$ amkan di tudert-nne$.

Mi ara neqqim seddaw useklu-nne$, newâa abrid n taddart, nettmuqul wid yettâeddayen. Gar-asen, yella yiwen, mi ara d-iâeddi s ukerrus-ines ad a$-d-yeoo a$ebar. Muê Lulu i d isem-is, yiwen umeâfun deg-s, maççi imi d bu imelyan kan, amdan-agi, seg wid-nni s-iqqaren êala nutni i yettidiren di ddunit.

Maççi d tiyita, At taddart akk ssnen tixidas-is. Idrimen $ur-s ayen din, d acu kan, akken meqqer loib-is i meqqer dd$el deg wul-is, akken gemmun yidrimen-is i igemmu yilem deg walla$-is. Acu-t wassen, nruê $ur-s ad d-ibzer ciî ad nexdem yiwet tes$unt s tmazi$t di tdukla tadelsant n taddart, ad twehmem, ur a$-d-iâriv ara ula $er waman, deg ugaraj-is i $-d-immuger,inna-d:

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 101 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

- … I$erdayen am kenwi teb$am ad tkellxem fell-i… tamazi$t-agi-nwen… ammer ad d-tegri deg ufus-iw ad tt-rbu$ anda ur d-tettban… êemdulleh mazal irgazen, hatan Si Butefliqa… yewwi-d ûûwab, êala netta kan i d debb-nwen…

D wagi i d Muê Lulu, d amerkanti gar Imazi$en ! Aîas i yellan am netta gar-ane$. Assen mi d-neffe$ si têanut-is, neddebdeb seg yimeslayen i $-d-yenna, deg iv-nni, amek nexdem i wakken ad d-nekkes zâaf ; nesse$res-as rrwadi n ukamyun-nni i d-yu$ d amaynut. Akamyun-nni, ur yelêi ara ddurt s lekmal-is, ussan-nni, d asbendeg, nett$ima seddaw useklu-nne$ di talwit, imi mi ara d-iâeddi ukamyun-nni zik, nettêulfu i teblavin-nni ttergigint.

# Aseklu n teméi

- 102 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Aseklu, $ef akken d-nnan imezwura, seg wasmi d-tecfa ddunit, yella di taddart. D im$aren, mi ten-nesteqsa qqaren-a$-d :

- Akka kan i t-id-ufan, ur igmi ur inqis.

Di tegrawla-nni-nne$, $ef akken d-êkan, êuzant-id Irumyen s lmina, yufeg umersun seg-s, yeqqim acêal iseggasen d ameâlal, yefra îîrad tu$al-d tefsut, teqqel-it-id tudert. Muê Lulu, yeb$a-yas lmut, yiwen wass yesuter tajmaât ad as-d-ternu kra n wakal ad yebnu igarajen i yikumya-ines, ters tiîî-is $ef uâerqub-nni ideg d-yem$i useklu n teméi. Maççi akka yal ass maca assen, teddukel taddart $ef yiwen wawal.

Neîeqen-d akk medden, wa deffir wa, awal d yiwen ; d awez$i, d lmuêal, ad s-nserreê i useklu. Tefra taluft yuoew-d Muê Lulu rregmat $er yiri-s. Seg wassen icuêen-a$ icuêen at taddart.

Ulamek ara s-nserreê i useklu, yid-s i truê teméi-nne$, limer ad teérem, ad twehmem, nweccem-it akk, nura fell-as ismawen-nne$ d yismawen n tid ized$en ulawen-nne$, nenoer fell-as ulawen. Ula d amezruy n JSK, ad t-tafem fell-as.

Aseklu-nne$ yerfed akk timucuha-nni n tayri, d amwanes, d ameddakel, yal wa deg-ne$ yeooa fell-as azgen n tudert-is. Ulamek ara s-nanef ! Yiwen yiv, rrâud, igeffuren, medden akk deg yixxamen. Nesla i ûûut amzun d ûûelêa. Azekka-nni mi d-nekker, d tazla, nufa-d di taddart ioadarmiyen, yekker waé-akkin ! D acu yevran ? D Muê Lulu, isker-d iv-nni, am akken iwulef, iédem s ukerrus-is yeffe$ abrid, iwet-itt $er useklu.

Yevra wayen ivran :

- Isker Muê Lulu
- Iqleâ aseklu
- Yemmut Muê Lulu
- I$av-iyi kan Useklu

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 103 -
Tegzem-as amrar d sser

Ramdane LASHEB

Yella yiwen umedyaz iêerr yiwet teqcict, inna-as i yemma-s :

- £ur-m taqcict-agi ad tt-tefkev ad teddu d tislit, teâjeb-iyi, ad tili d zzwao-iw. Terra-as yemma-s n teqcict :
- Yirbaê a mmi, kkes a$bel ad k-terou.

Ar tagara seg iruê urgaz-nni $er l$erba yemma-s n teqcict-nni t$emmeq tegzem-as amrar d sser, texdeâ-it, tefka-tt i wayev. Mi d-yusa umdyaz-nni si l$erba yufa-d taqcict-nni deg uxxam-is tezweo. Yemma-s n teqcict-nni, yu$al amzun maççi d winna, ur tecliâ ara akk deg-s. Ssyin iwwi asefru yenna-as :

- Aql-i seddaw inijwel
- Lmakla-w d tizwel
- Idda-yi usennan weêd-i
- Balak wi ittamnen tuooel
- D lqum n teooel
- Mi s-nnan awal ad tefdi
- Tefka-yas-ten deg ufenoal
- Ad iîîes deg inijel
- Alamma ihder i Rebbi

Lêan acu lêan iwwev-d lweqt ad terbu teqcict-nni, tehlek ulac anda ur tt-wwin ara ur as-d-ufin ddwa.

Yemma-s - 104 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

n teqcict temmekta-d amedyaz-nni, tenna-yas, ahat, ivfer-itt-id wul-is, ad ruêe$ $ur-s, ad velbe$ deg-s ad d-yas, ad s-isemmeê, ahat ddwa $ur-s i yella.

Assen, yemma-s teroa alarmi iffe$ urgaz n yelli-s, truê tessawel i umedyaz-nni. Iwwev-d, yaf-itt-id tetteqliliê di tesga. Mi tt-iwala akken di liêala-nni t$av-it nezzeh yenna-yas :

- Leâmer ur t-inqis ur t-irad
- A tuzyint wer ttagad
- Seg wul-im kkes ttexmim
- Ay aênin ay ajewwad
- A feteê muhab
- Tekksev i tuzyint le$mim
- Tarwiêt atta di lêisab
- Taqcict tenneâtab
- A ccix Muêend U Lêusin

Akken ifuk asefru-s, taqcict tu$was tebda la tnehhi d lweqt ad terbu. Iffe$ umedyaz, tessawel yemma-s i tlawin ad tt-âiwnent rebbu n yelli-s.

Mi d-ikcem urgaz-is tameddit yufa, yerna $ur-s uqcic, tameîîut-is ur tt-yu$ wara. Argaz iwhem deg wayen ittwali. Mi isteqsa amek akka ! Taveggalt-is terra-as-id :

- D leflani i wumi d-nessawel, iwala-tt kan d$a Rebbi ifka-d liser.
- Akken ifuk wagur inna-as urgaz-nni i tmeîîut-is :

Netta iffe$ $er ssuq, $er lqevyan, nettat teffe$ $er tala ad d-tagem aman. Mi d-tu$al si tala, tâedda-d $ef tejmaât tufa-d amedyaz-nni, iqqim $ef udekkan, aqerru-s gar ifassen-is.

# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Mi tewwet ad tâeddi issevfer-as asefru, yenna-as :

- Lâeslama-m si tala
- Leâyun n tnila
- Taîîucin bêal leêcic
- Ëemduleh mi teêliv
- Mebruk
- Nseâdam aqcic

Yusa-d urgaz-is si ssuq, teftel seksu, tesseww aksum i yimensi. Alarmi d lawan ideg ara yeçç imensi inna-as urgaz-is heggi-d imensi. Tameîîut tessers-d tlata n tbaqyin n seksu d uksum, tenna-as :

1. Atan dayen ihegga imensi.

Argaz iddem-d tacekkart n ssem ismar kra di ttnaûfa n yiwet n tbaqit inna-as i tmeîîut-is :

1. Anef-asent i tbaqyin-agi, akken llant. Tura ad ruêe$ ad ssiwle$ i leflani. Argaz iruê $er tejmaât issawel-d i umedyaz.

Akken d-ççuren tawwurt, argaz izwar-d, amedyaz deffir-s, tbedd tmeîîut-is tenna i urgaz-is :

1. Ay argaz di leânaya-k, ma ur iyi-teooiv ad d-awi$ asefru !

Imiren ma ihwa-ak xas en$-iyi !

Yenna-as urgaz-is :

- Ad yeg Rebbi teççiv aqerru-m ! Ini-d.

Tenna-as :

- Ttxilek a lbaz meééiyen
- A win itâeffan
- Ruê asif enz-as $ef rrif
- D lâibad i d imcumen
- Äewwlen ad k-$edren
- £ef zzwao-is êedd ur t-iîîif

# Afḍam

# Salah SAIDI

Yeḍleq-d yiḍ i weɛlaw-is ɣef taddart. Ikemmel areqqem n yigenni s yitran. Ters-d tsusmi alarmi ɣ-d-yewwi Ṛebbi d taddart n war imezdaɣ am di tmucuha-nni tiqburin. Ur tselleḍ siwa i serru n waman, asqerqer n yimqerqyar ɣef yiri n yiɣẓer, rrkeḍ n lewḥuc, askeɛwew n wuccanen d weskerwec n yiferrawen n yisekla.

Deg uxxam i d-yezgan di tlemmast n taddart-agi, yiwen ilemẓi yebded zdat usfaylu iruḥ am wakken yurez-it lḥir, udem-is werraɣ am win isumm uzrem, tafekka-s tulwa amzun ɣlin-d fell-as yineẓman n talsa. Ɣas ulamma di taddart i yella, ul-is yeǧǧa-t-in di tmanaɣt : yemmekti-tt-id...

Yemmekti-d tagnit n lfiraq d tin ukud yessarem ad yezdi axxam. D yelli-s n tfamilt akken qqaren. Iɛedda wesmekti zdat wallen-is am usaru, yemmekti-d ussan n tesdawit i sɛeddan deg uẓeṭṭa n weɛlaw n yimmal-nsen : iger-d nnehta, ad s-tiniḍ teffeɣ-d seg udrar n tmess.

Yurew-d yimi-s takufit yimetman, yerra-ten ɛeddan deg ugerjum-is am yibursen n ǧǧaj. Iḥulfa imir-nni s urkam agensi yebɣa ad yeṭṭerḍeq, tusa-d ɣer-s tekti n uɣewweɣ d useɣres n yimurar d yensayen yehtutan.

Amek ara yeqbel asaḍuf adanki? Ad yaɣ yelli-s n ɛemmi-s i yeḥseb am weltma-s werǧin iḥulfa ɣer-s s wayen umi qqaren tayri. Ixemmem ad yerwel seg ufus n lmektub maca yuɣal ibeddel rray-is mi d-yemmekti iman-is d awḥid n snat tfekkiwin yeẓẓlen di tesga, i yefkan fell-as ussan n temẓi-nsent.

Imir i yegzem usunded-is s usiwel n ladan n tafrara. Dɣa ixemmel i yiɣallen-is d yiḍarren-is ad yaɣ luḍu ad yeẓẓal…

- 108 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008

# Si Muḥend iferrun timsal

# Boudjema AZIRI

Nassawev-as rreêma i Aéar Rabaê (1907-2004) i $-d-yewwin asefru-agi n Si Muêend U Mêend ur nettwassen ara $er wid d-yuran isefra-ines, am Bulifa, Ferâun d Mâemmri.

Si Muêend d win iteddun aîas; tamurt n leqbayel inuda-tt tardast tardast, tudrin-is yessen-itent d tirni. Yiwen wass yewwi-t lmektub $er yiwet taddart ur ccfi$ ara $ef yisem-is.

Tameddit n wass, akken yezzewre$ yiîij, yeqqim $ef teblaî n loameâ, d acu n llebsa, d acu n lêala, yessusem ur yessin yiwen. Akken yebda yettna$ yiv d wass, ibded-d $ur-s yiwen uqcic yenna-yas:

- Iceggeâ-iyi-d xali ad k-âerve$ $er imensi ay inebgi n Rebbi. Xali-s n uqcic-agi d argaz lâali, yefka azal amuqqran i wawal, ma yewâed ur yettxalaf, ma yeggul ur iêennet. Muqader $er medden merra s cci-s, s lêerma-s d nnif-is... Maâna txuûû-it yiwet t$awsa. Tekka-as-d s$ur Rebbi, ur yesâi ara aqcic ara t-iwerten. Tameîîut-is d tiqcicin kan i d-tettarew; setta teqcicin ta deffir ta!
- Mi terfed s tadist tis sebâa, yeffe$-as-d limin:
- Tikkelt-agi ma ilul-d $ur-i uqcic, atan tennebra tmeîîut-iw ma ur zli$ ara ikerri yesâan sebâa n turdas deg wacciwen-is. Yu$ lêal tameîîut-is imiren i d aggur-is. Kra n wussan kan yerna-d $ur-s uqcic! Anda ara k-rren $er lferê; ti$ratin, îîbel ireddex... Ass n sbuâ ilaq ad yezlu ikerri yesâan sebâa turdas deg wacciwen-is, ne$ ma ulac, tameîîut-is ad tennebru.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 111 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Ddurt kamel u netta d anadi. Kra n ssuq yellan yewwev-it. D awez$i ad yaf ikerri bu sebâa turdas deg wacciwen-is! Afrag-is yeççur d akraren bernen wacciwen-nsen maca yiwen ur yessawev sebâa turdas. Ass-nni d aneggaru akken ad yebru i tmeîîut-is, ad s-d-teoo mmi-s d aleqqaq, aqcic-nni i$ef yessefna tarwiêt. Ijmeâ-d akk lâuqqal, imrabven d lmacayex, iveggef-iten-id, yesteqsa-ten yiwen yiwen akken ad s-d-afen tawwurt; ur iberru ara i tmeîîut-is... Ulac!

àçan swan... Fkan-d awal-nsen aneggaru:

- Ad yemmzel ikerri bu sebâa turdas deg wacciwen-is ne$ ad tennebru tmeîîut ma ur yeb$i ara urgaz ad yeênet.

Akken yesla s yiwen uâervi yensa di loameâ, iceggeâ $ur-s akken ad yeçç imensi... yerna ad yawi deg-s ttwab, yerna a t-yesteqsi “wi éran? ad yeârev tiwwura n Rebbi!”

Akken i d-yekcem Si Muê, s uçamar, llebsa taqdimt, yeêûa dayen ifuk îîmeâ!

Yeçça Si Muê imensi, teqqel-it-id terwiêt, yenîeq $er bab n uxxam:

- D acu i k-yu$en ay argaz lâali... a nettkel $ef Rebbi a d-yefk tifrat.

Kra yellan din îîalen-d $ur-s... Inna umedyaz:

Allah tiliv g lâewn-ik

Nekni akk d arraw-ik

Taqcict $ef tizi inebran

Yeggul wergaz wer yeênit

Leêram ikreh-it

Izeâm-it-id cciîan

Ïîef-d mmi-s deg irebbi-s

Tqissev ccebr-is

Ma yella ddnub a t nemâawan

Ma nemmuqel amek yefra Si Muêend tamsalt-agi iweâren aîas, $as akken lâuqqal akked lecyax i teâna taluft tban-asen-d tifrat-is d awez$i, ad nefhem belli Si Muêend d win yezwaren loil-ines s waîas di tmusni.

Yeffe$ deg tmu$li-

- 112 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

nni-nsen tadeyqant, iééer tikufa akken llant d ûûeê, s walla$ d ilelli. £ur Si Muêend, taqsiî-agi n berru $ef loal n te$zi n wacciwen n ikerri, d limin n lêanet ur t-iqebbel ara leâqel-is. Ayagi d cciîan kan i t-yeb$an... “Izeâm-it-id cciîan”.

# Ameɛɛen

# Ahmed HAMOUM

Imdanen mgaraden. Ibva-ten Rebbi d leûnaf ; wa yerbeê wa yerzeê. Wa yesâa wa yexla. Wa yertaê wa yevreê. Wa yefhem wa yeggugem...

Tagi, $ef yiwen urgaz ttxelliûen-t medden imi i sen-ineqq iâdawen-nsen. Mcawaren fell-as kra n yirgazen, sxedmen-d yiwen umeddakel-is ukkud içça tagella d lemleê ; sse$wan-t s yidrimen. Isnubget-it s imensi i wakken ad d-asen wid ara t-yen$en. Tameîîut teêûa s wayen d-ihegga urgaz-is. Imi ur teb$i ara ad te$li temgervt deg uxxam-is lafe$ ad d-grin deg yimi, tekker $er mmi-s yellan di dduê, tezzuzun-it tettmeââin :

A uccen gar wuccanen

Iv-agi ad iwêel wuccen-ik

Teqqarev i medden êerce$

I iêercen deg tmital-ik !

A win ($e)f i rsen yidrimen

A lâali êader iman-ik

Tameîîut tettcewwiq trennu ; ameârav yefhem lmeâna, yewwet wul-is yexcawet imi yeéra ayen i t-yettrajun, d$a yessuter seg wat uxxam aman akken ad ya$ luvu ; nnan-as :

- Ïîâam yezwar tiéilla.

Inebgi igguma ad yeçç alma yeééul. Mi s-ççuren ssvel, yeffe$ $er ddaw lêara, yessenser, yerra ssyin yeslek.

- 114 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Tayev $ef urgaz-iven umi d-heggan taxazabit akken ad t-n$en. Yiwen umedyaz ur idrig kra $ef tiî-is, yekkat s lemâun i wakken ad t-issefhem ad yerwel :

- Ay abujad wer neârif
- £urek iûeggaden ad k-êewsen
- S ufella heddren llsan
- Tacerket s wadda i tt-kersen
- Abudid ma ad d-iger lexrif !

Ma illa seg w(id) itâerrfen Imi iâedda fell-as uzaylal ; ur yefhim ara lmeâna, yettwan$a. Akka i tverru d bu niyya ur nteddu d yiman-is. Yal mi ara tevru tedyant yecban ta, ttawin-d tsirrit-a :

- Uêdiq ifehhem s timmi,
- ma d ungif ar das-nini.

# Nna Ḥǧila

# Hacène HALOUANE

Seg wasmi i d-cfi$ i yiman-iw, Nna Ëeoila tella tama-w, amzun d yemma tis snat. Qqaren d nettat i yi-igezmen timiî. Maççi ala nekkini. Tizyiwin-iw merra d wid i yi-yugaren cwiî âeddan-d $ef ufus-is. Thucc-iten, tecrew-iten, tettel-iten, tectedduy-iten, teîîef-asen afus ad gren taqejjirt.

Nna Ëeoila zuret. Avar-is d asagem. Ddmuj-is d llufan yufan. Segmi i s-d-cfi$ ur tbeddel : ur tcab -$as ma tcab wi i yeéran ? imi aqerru-yis yezga i$umm- ur yekmic wudem-is.

Seg wasmi i d-cfi$ i yiman- iw, qqaren-d tesâa aqcic d teqcict. Taqcict deg uxxam-is ad tt-ihenni Öebbi, aqcic di Lezzayer, -ur ten-ssine$ imi leâmer ten-wala$ $ur-s uma nettat weroin tewwi-ten-id deg wawal- Akli d Jeooiga -akka i d ismawen-nsen, éran medden llan, amzun di tmucuha.

Am akken i d-qqaren Lmulud n at wadda d gma-s. Ssne$ Lmulud n at wadda, d tidet icuba-yas cwiî. Zur, berrik, acu wis d acu i t-ixuûûen i wakken ad yilwi$ wudem-is, ad tiênin tmu$li-s am tmu$li n weltma-s. Xaîi. Nna Ëeoila ur tesâa baba-s, ur tesâa gma-s, ur tesâa yelli-s wala mmi-s. D$a bitt argaz-is, yiwen ur s-d-yecfi armi ula d isem-is, yiwen ur t-yessin.

Nna Ëeoila tezde$ weêd-s, di tlemmast n taddart. £as akken si berra, am uxxam-is am yixxamen n wiyav. Mi ara tkecmev, d ayen nniven, mazal ttwali$-t gar wallen-iw, aêanu-nni $as qqen deg-s izgaren. Cfi$ nettemzazzal dinna. Mi ara muqle$ ass-agi, qqare$-as ahat d targit i tt-urga$ ne$

- 116 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

ahat d teméi-nni i nella meééiyit i yesme$ren axxam-nni gar wallen-nne$.

D tagi i d Nna Ëeoila. Iciwi-s yezga yeâmer : ma maççi d taêlawat ne$ d taêjurt n ssker d ini$man.

Tezwaray tiéevt zdat-s. A win i d-temlal deg-ne$, ad as-tesslef, ad terfed, ad as-teççar afus-is ternu-yas "Öebbi êrez".

Da$ netta ula d nekni, win ye$lin, win yennu$nan, win i wumi i yedda usennan, yazzel s irebbi n Nna Ëeoi. Din din, tesfev-as imeîîawen, tezzuzen-it imi arebbi n tyemmat yeâmer urâad yettaded yiwen mi ara d-yas wayev.

Ussan ttazzalen am wavu wa i d-deggir wa. Nettnerni, nettim$ur, ntettu. Nesâa ixxamen tura, nesâa dderya, nesâa i$eblan-nne$, xaîi mexîa n win mazal yettmekti-d irebbi n Nna Ëeoila. £as ma nekk, ar iv-a, lemmer ur dessen ara fell-i medden, ad as-$li$ deg yirebbi, ad ru$ cwiî gar ifassen-is, ad iyi-tesslef i uqerru-w. èri$, $urwat wi yi-d-isellen, $er ccib- iw.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 117 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Nna Ëeoila mazal-itt waêd-s, am zik. Lemmer di trebba akraren, ass-a tajlibt-is meqqret, imi d irgazen i trebba, attan waêd-s. Ass-a ur mazal ad tegzem timiî i yiwen. Qqaren "wis ifassen-is ma zeddigit ?" uma yella sbiîar dinna irebbunt tlawin ass-agi. Timqessin n Nna Ëeoila yuli-tent svav, $as akken mazal-itt axxam ittak-itt i wayev, da ad testeqsi $ef um$ar, da $ef llufan yuvnen, da aîas ayagi ur tâedda, tejjem-iten kan. Ad teqqim zdat n tewwurt, ad as-fken afenoal n lqahwa, ad temmekti zik-nni, ad tevs cwiî, syinna ad tennejmeâ $er texxamt-is, ula d trisiti ur tt-tessekcem am nettat am wiyav, s wacu ara tt-tettxellis ? Da$ nettat ur tettêar ara ad tu$al $er dinna, tettwali-t amzun d aéekka.

Yelli-s, tura arraw-is d irgazen, tettmekti-tt-id kan mi ara teêwio amwanes. Mulac ad k-ihenni Rebbi ihenni-ya$. Mmi-s, ar ass-a d isem kan, yiwen ur yessin udem-is. Ma d at taddart, buh, wi iqevâen iman-is ar d-ilhu d wiyav-nni.

Akken kan ara yali wass, ad t$iwel ad d-teffe$ seg "uéekka-s" ad tezzu$ur iman-is, $as ma mazal-itt tqeîîeb. Mazal imectaê êemmlen ad tt-walin tusa-d. D acu maççi am zik, $as tiêlawatin rran-t tiqit, afus ara yesselfen ulac win i t-yerwan. Sin akken, i yettali i yettubbu alamma ye$li-d îîlam.

D acu ara yerren ameêbus $er lqebs-is ? Tettagad i tt-yetta$en, weêd-s, alamma traê-d. Teéra ddunit tbeddel, ulac anwa ara d-yasen ad yesteqsi fell-as, ma yella ur d-tban ara.

Armi d assen tameddit n wass. Ageffur seg yigenni si tmurt. Ïîlam imvelles tûub s axxam-is, tessen iûeddaren n webrid am akken d nettat i ten-inejren, tetteddu s leêder, akussar, taéayt, aéatav, yeccev udar-is. Têulfa i tmeccact-is tennûel, teqqi-d $ef yiman-is t$umm ivarren-is, tûeggem acemmal-is. Tessawel, abrid, berdayen "Ay abbuh ay at laârav !" Yu$ lêal yiwen si loiran-is imaren i d-yennejmaâ, yesla i te$ri, yessawel ula d netta i medden.

Tamecwart akka nnejmaâent-d fell-as tlawin, zzint-as, ta la tettaârav ad tt-terfed, ta teqqar-as "Ur ttagad". Uzzlen yirgazen, wwin-d acceîîiv ideg ara tt-awin $er sbiîar. Tenna-asen :

- Arout, b$i$ ad sle$ i umeooed uqbel ad ruêe$ !
- Wi$ef ara nmeooed ? i s-nnant tlawin i s-d-yezzin.

118 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Meoodemt fell-i, éri$ ur d ttu$ale$ ara, taruéi n win meqqren, d taruéi n ubuqal, ugade$ mi ara yi-d-awin, ulac win ara imeooden fell-i. Ahamt a tilawin, b$i$ ad t-awi$ deg umeééu$-iw.

Lehwa la tekkat, bu tkerrust la yettraou. Irgazen ffren aceîîiv mulac ad yebzeg. Tilawin refdent ti$ri. Nna Ëeoila di tlemmast tefreê, tevsa, tenna "A kent-yeâfu Rebbi".

Refden-tt yirgazen, $awlen yis-s. Tilawin nnejmaâent $er yixxamen-nsent. Nettat ala rrwaê n wass-nni. Tikwal, mi ara qqime$ zdat n tewwurt n uxxam-is, iwerra-yi-d Rebbi, ttwali$ Nna Ëeoila tettali-d tiseddarin-nni zdat-i.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 119 -
# Tala iḥulfan

# Youcef MERAHI

Aql-iyi ass-a d inebgi n tala iḥulfan. Tala iḥulfan ! Lebni n wawal-agi tlaq-as tɣimit. Maca win yufan awal-agi ad s-rreɣ tajmilt.

Amek tettḥulfu tala amek yettḥulfu wemdan ? Tala tesserwa-yaɣ aman maca nettarra tajmilt i wayeḍ. Akka ihi tala tetteẓẓem iman-is i wakken ad tidir tudert. Ma d amdan meskin aḥulfu-ines ibeddu-d ass n tlalit-is. Llufan mi ara d-brarḥent wallen-is yettɛeggiḍ. Amek akka ? A d-nqabel tudert s imeṭṭawen ? Ih ! Akka. Ass amezwaru n tlalit-nneɣ yugguni-t ass aneggaru, asmi ara d-testeqsi tucmitt-nni i wakken ad aɣ-tezzuɣer war lebɣi-nneɣ ɣer umaḍal n at laxert. Akka i d ddunit !

Simmal tettfeggiḍ tala, simmal aman-is neqqsen, simmal aḥulfu-ines irennu. Simmal yettidir wemdan, simmal tazmert-is tettanqas, simmal aḥulfu-ines yettimɣur. D acu iciddi yellan gar wemdan d tala ? Ayagi d tamsalt i yeɛnan tafelsafit neɣ tazemnit.

D acu i yessimɣuren aḥulfu n wemdan ? D timetti. Acku timetti tebna ɣef yal taɣawsa yebdan si lemliḥ armi d alexxax. Akka amdan inejjer abrid-is anida yessexṣar tikwal, anida yesseqɛad tikwal. Dagi d tikerkas. Dagi d lexdaɛ. Dagi d acmumeḥ. Dagi d imeṭṭi. Dagi d ssɛaya. Dagi tigguylelt. Dagi d laẓ. Dagi d tawant. Dagi d karuh. Dagi d tayri.

Aḥulfu n wemdan yebna yal ass ɣef tayri. Win teǧǧa tayri yessureg ayen yellan deg wul-is. Amek tebɣam ad yidir wemdan d wemdan, ad tettwabna timetti bla tayri ?

- 120 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

tebɣam ad yeddu wemḍal bla tayri ? D acu n liḥala n wergaz neɣ n tmeṭṭut teffeɣ tayri ?

Maca tayri mačči d učči. Yal yiwen deg-neɣ akken it t-yettwali. Wihin yetturar s tayri am win ineqqen akud; yerra-tt kan i thuski. Wagi yeṭṭafar kan icuḍaḍ n lxalat, yeqqar-as nekk “ḥemmleɣ”. Wayeḍ nniḍen iguber tayri ur tt-yewwiḍ.

Ma d wihin yerra-tt i ucali si tezniqt ɣer tayeḍ, taxriṭ teččur, la yettsawam di tayri. Yella wayeḍ tin iwala iḥemmel-itt. Maca nekk mmugreɣ-d tayri taḥeqqanit ala di tmedyazt d yedlisen i yessalayen tayri ɣer tegnawt.

Ccix Lḥesnawi d Faḍma. Aragon d Elsa. Qays d Layla. D wiyaḍ nniḍen merra. Ih ! Roméo d Juliette. Tristan d Iseult. Anda telliḍ a Werther ? I Jamil anda yella ? Lɛenqa d Leḥmam ? Wigi uran ɛacen ẓran jerrben weznen walan meyzen muqlen… ḥulfan s tayri, ḥulfan i tayri.

Nekk, ahbuh i nekk ! D acu-yi zdat n wigi ? D amdan. Ḥulfaɣ ula d nekkini. Uriɣ ula d nekkini. Aneggaru deg-sen : “Wehran, tafesna 31”. Ammud-agi n isefra yebren tamgerṭ i tikti n tayri. Acku tayri n war tiririt mačči d tayri : d atihi.

Deg wedlis-agi-inu d wiyaḍ i uriɣ, cuddeɣ tikti-inu n tayri ɣer yismawen-nni i d-bedreɣ usawen. I yurgaɣ tayri ur d-nelli ! Anda-kem a yemma ?

Nekk, ahbuh i nekk ! Zegreɣ akin i xemsin (lukan di ddiminu aql-i kecmeɣ i lemliḥ). Maca mazal ttarguɣ tayri. Sani tessufuɣ tayri am tagi ? Tessufuɣ ɣer webrid ireglen, ɣer ṭṭaq n tisselbi, ɣer wesṭerḍeq n wul, ɣer ɛawaz n llyali, ɣer taruẓi n tuɣmas, ɣer umeǧǧed n iḍudan, ɣer temlel n uqerru, ɣer taḍsa tasemmaṭ, ɣer tira n wurfan, ɣer ɛeggu n wass, ɣer wezdaɣ n usteqsi, ɣer tarewla zdat tilawt, ɣer tatut n tummast…

Ihi a tala iḥulfan rnu ẓẓeg-d si tmaẓẓagin-im, efk-aɣ-d aman i tissit d usired, atan wul yumes.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 121 -

- 122 -                             Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008

# Tihawt tazayzant n tmaziɣt

# Zahir MEKSEM

Iswi n umagrad-a d awal ɣef useqdec s wudem nniḍen n tira. Ad yerzu tatɣult iɣer ur nezzi ara tiṭ s tuget. Asentel-is yerza tihawt tazayzant neɣ tirant n tmaziɣt (Présence publique ou graphique de tamazight). S umata, ur llint ara aṭas n tezrawin ɣef usentel am wa. Ihi awal-iw ad yili aṭas d aglam, d tamawin.

Iseqsiyen ɣef ara yili umeslay d wi :

Seg wasmi d-isuḍ waḍu n tlelli d tugdut ɣef Lezzayer, aseggas n 1988 d asawen, tamaziɣt tekcem ɣer tesdawit akked uɣebaz, tuɣal d tutlayt taɣelnawt ; nezmer ad d-nini ldint tewwura i useqdec n tmaziɣt. Deg wayen yerzan tihawt-is tirant :

"Tamaziɣt tban-d deg twennaḍt aṭas n yiseggasen-aya. Sqedcen-tt yimdanen akken ad d-seknen yes-s udem n twennaḍt. Syin akin, cwiṭ, cwiṭ teṭṭef imukan-nniḍen. Aseqdec-is, ihi, yebda seg yiseggasen imezwura seld tilelli n tmurt. Maca lawan-nni teqqim kan d tira ɣef leḥyuḍ, ɣef tesfifin, ɣef yiḍebsiyen" 27

D acu, deg wayen yerzan tilin-is deg tmetti, aṭas n yiseqsiyen i d-icudden ɣur-s, amedya :

- Ma tettwaseqdec tmaziɣt deg twennaḍt ?

27 Z. Meksem, 2005, Les langues des écrits urbains dans la ville de Béjaia : Qu’en pensent les jeunes apprenants de tamazight », In M. Rispail (Sous dir) avec la collaboration de N.Tigziri, Langues maternelles : contacts, variations et enseignement. Le cas de la langue amazighe, Paris, Harmattan, Pp. 205 -215.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 125 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

- Anda ara tt-naf ?

- S wanta tira s tettwaru ?

(Zemren ad ilin yiseqsiyen-nniḍen yerzan asentel-a, maca d wid i yesran i tezrawin d tsestanin deg unnar akken ad sɛun tiririt tussnant iwatan).

Iseqsiyen-a yakk, s umata, d wid yerzan taɣult n tesnilesmetti (sociolinguistique). Tririt fell-asen, ad aɣ-d-temmel azal d umkan n tutlayt n tmaziɣt, mačči kan anagar ayen i d-icudden ɣer uẓayer-is asertan, maca, tirirt-a ad aɣ-d-temmel daɣen amkan-is d tixutert-is ɣer yimsulɣa (wid i tt-yettmeslayen). Deg wannect-a ad negzu azal n tutlayt yettilli-d ɣef sin n wudmawen.

Deg tama ayen akk i d-icudden ɣer usɣiwes utlayan (planification linguistique). Wi rzan adabu, s wawal-nniḍen d netta i ilan allalen akken ad yefk tagnit i tutlayt akken ad tennerni, akken ad taɣ amdiq i tt-iwatan : ama deg yiɣerbazen, deg tedbelt, deg wallalen n teywalt, atg. Dɣa, ma nmuqel tamaziɣt ass-a, ad naf aẓayer-is ibeddel aṭas, ur teqqim ara d tutlayt taddayt (langue basse), ma nserwes-itt d taɛrabt tantalant, acku tamaziɣt tuɣal d tutlayt taɣelnawt, tekcem ɣer yiɣerbazen, tekcem ɣer taɣulin n teywalt.

Maca ayen yerzan aslugen-is 28 (sa standadisation) teqqim war tifrat, amedya ar ass-a ulac ayen yellan d unsib ara yesddaklen tira-s, amawal-is. Annect-a daɣen yeqqen srid ɣer wahil asertan n udabu; d netta i yesɛan azref akken ad yefru tamsalt-a.

Deg tama-nniḍen, asnerni n tutlayt yasɛa assaɣ d ameqqran d tmetti ideg tella. Tigensas, timuɣliwin, tiktiwin n yimdanen ɣef tutlayt-nsen ttilin d tasalelt tameqqrant, ttakkent afud ameqqran i tutlayt akken ad teddu ɣer zdat. Anadi deg taɣult-a yessukkus-d amek ttwalin yimdanen tutlayt-nsen, ma bɣan ad tt-ɣren, ma bɣan ad tt-arun. S umata ma bɣan ad tili, ad tidir. Tin ɣur-s, annect-a yeskan-d daɣen tuṭṭfa-nsen deg tutlayt-a imi tutlayt tettidir s lebɣi n wid i tt-yettmeslayen.

28 - Aslugen ila anamek n "noramalisation" sqedceɣ-t s unamek n "la standardiastion" akken ad d-segziɣ ayen i wimi tesra tmaziɣt ass-a akka am : yiwen n umawal, yiwen n ugemmay, yiwet n tirawalt.

- 126 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Tudert-a tettili s useqdec-is deg yal taɣult. (Amedya tagnit-a i yas-yettunfken deg tesɣunt-a). Aya yebɣa ad d-yini, tutlayt yewwi-d ad tili, ama d tira, ama d timawt deg yal adeg, deg yal akud anda tezmer ad tettwaseqdec.

Deg wayen yerzan tira, tamezwarut dayen ibanen, d amenzay ɣer medden merra, tira i d iman, i d tazmert, i d tudert n tutlayt. Acku ayen yuran ur inegger ara, ur yettnejli ara, ur t-tekkat ara tatut. Yewwi-d ad nẓer d nettat ara yerren azal i tmaziɣt. Mammeri, yura deg udlis (Inna-yas- Ccix Muḥen): "Di lqern n ɛecrin ideg nella, tussna telḥa […] Ihi, yezmer umdan ad yessexdem allalen-is […] Ass-a nezmer ad d-nessufeɣ idlisen di mkul ssenf " 29.

Am wakken i d-yura deg udlis (Les poèmes kabyles anciens): "Tura tamussni tuɣal s idlisen. Degmi uriɣ adlis-a i keč d tezyiwin-ik, ad ak-d-yeqqim d tigejdit i usenned, d tigejdit i lebni " 30.

Tin ɣur-s, ula deg umennuɣ n Umussu Adelsan Amaziɣ (MCB), seg zik awal i d-yettuɣalen, nnig n umennuɣ asertan, d tira, d afares, d assufeɣ n yidlisen, akken ad teqqim tutlayt, akken ad as-yettunefk yisem n tutlayt, ur tettɣimi ara kan d tantala.

Tamaziɣt ass-a teṭṭef aṭas n yimedqan, teskuṭṭef-d deg yal amkan, yennerna ciṭ uẓayer-is, tettcali deg yiberdan, teṭṭef iɣerban, tekcem tanezzut. S wawal awezlan, ad d-nini ur teḥjib ara, ur teffir ara. Aṭas n tegnatin ideg d-ttbin. D annect-a iwimi qqaren tihawt tazayzant neɣ tihawt tirant (Présence publique, présence graphique). S wawal-nniḍen, anamek-is d tilin n tutlayt, d tudert n tutlayt deg twennaḍt.

# Amek i d-yettili waya ?

Tihawt n tutlayt tettili deg twennaḍt ticki imdanen ttarun-tt deg yal amkan ideg tezmer ad tili, semrasent d allal n usissen neɣ d allal n usussen (publicité), amedya: ismawen akk n wayen yerzan:

29- M.Mammeri, 199, Inna-yas Ccix Muḥend, Paris, Maspéro, asebter 15.

30- M.Mammeri, 1988, Les poèmes kabyles anciens, Paris, Maspéro, asebter 60.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 127 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

a- tanezzut, akka am :

- tiḥunna, leqhawi, allalen n tumnayt, igalisen akken bɣun ilin,
- isufar n wučči neɣ n usired (lgazuz, lqahwa, lgaṭu, cukula, sabun, rriḥa atg.).
- Tisfifin, iḍebsiyen, C.D, iɣmisen. Ddwa…

b- tisuddwin, akka am :

- tinedlisin, tisdawiyin, tisnawiyin, tiɣiwanin, lwilayat,
- iɣerbazen, tidukliwin, ikabaren, tizrigin…

c- tiɣawsiwin-nniḍen, akka am :

- tikerḍwin n uncad, SMS, internet, iẓekwan, tira ɣef yiɣerban (graffitis)…

D acu i azal n tihawt n tutlayt deg twennaḍt ?

- - Tamezwarut, tezmer ad tili d aferdis n usnekwu (élément identificateur) n twennaḍt-nni. S tira ad nẓer d acu i d tutlayt n tmetti-nni
- - Tis snat, temmal-d azal i tefka tmetti i tutlayt-is, ma bɣan ad tili, ma ṭṭfen deg-s, ma ḥemmlen ad tt-walin, s wannect-a ara d-senfalin tigensas-nsen ɣef tutlayt i fernen gar tiyiḍ. S tewzel n wawal tettak-d issalen ɣef wassaɣ yellan gar tutlayt d tmetti.
- - Tis kraḍ, tihawt-a tezmer ad tili d aɣbalu s ara yelmed umdan amawal d tira n tutlayt acku simmal yettwali, simmal yesseqsay, simmal ilemmed.

Aseqsi i d-icudden ɣer wayen yezrin d wa : S wanta tira s ttarun yemdanen deg tegnatin-a ?

Uqbel ad d-nerr ɣef useqsi-ya, yewwi-d ad nẓer deg Lezzayer llan yisuḍaf (leqwanen) i d-yessufeɣ udabu ɣef usexdem n tutlayin deg twennaḍt. Leqwanen-a qqnen ɣer tsertit n useɛreb. Deg useggas 1981, yella le décrét n° 6136 du 15 mars, iwimi semman "Arabisation de l’environnement", tallit-nni i d-lulen kra n yismawen n tmura ffɣen akk i yidles d tesmidegt (la toponymie) n tmurt-a.

Amedya : (Buleyda, wihran, qusenṭina, Sukeykida).

Syina ulsen-as-d i usaḍuf-nni deg useggas n 1998, yerna sḍefren-as-d lexṭiyat i kra n win ara yarun s tutlayt-nniḍen.

Maca, ɣas ffɣen-d leqwanen-a, deg twennaḍt, deg tedbelt, deg

- 128 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

luzinat, lbankat… mazal yezga useqdec n tefransist. R. Kahlouche, iga snat n tsastanin (enquêtes) deg temdint n Tizi Uzzu, yiwet 1996, tayeḍ 2000, yufa gar snat n talliyin-a, imdanen uɣalen ttarun aṭas s tefransist ugar taɛrabt, ugar tamaziɣt. Yewweḍ ɣer tamawt-a :

"Deg useggas n 2000, i tuget tefransist neɣ i yuɣalen medden ɣer tefransist ayen i wimi yesssemma "la refrancisation de l’environnement " 31.

Ma deg wayen yerzan tamaziɣt, ulac lqanun i d-yeqqaren ilaq ad tt-nesseqdec, am wakken ulac lqanun i tt-igedlen. Ma nmuqel ad naf aṭas n yismawen n tmaziɣt yellan deg twennaḍt d ddewla i ten-yuran.

# Tira n tmaziɣt deg twennaḍt

Deg twennaḍt amur ameqqran seqdacen talaṭinit, d acu, deg sya ɣer da, ad naf daɣen tifinaɣ. Annect-a ad aɣ d-yessegzi, deg wayen yerzan tihawt n tmaziɣt d akken tura s tlaṭinit :

- d tin i yuɣen deg tmetti ;
- d tin i yugten deg twennaḍt ;
- talaṭinit d tin i fernen yemdanen i usissen n tɣawsiwin-nsen;
- talaṭinit d tin i yettwasmettin s waṭas (socialisée);
- tlaṭinit d tin i tesseqdac tmetti, ula d ddewla aṭas n yigalisen (plaques, enseignes) tura-ten s tlaṭinit.

Γef wannect-a ad d-nini, nnig n tmental i yefkan afud i ufran n tlaṭinit, tira-aya :

- tuɣ deg tmetti si zzman aqdim ;
- fessuset i ulmad d uselmed ;
- iɣbula yellan akk ttwarun s tlaṭinit ;
- tla ilugan n tira, d ayen yellan d agejdan acku ilugan d allal i yeǧǧan imdanen ad arun, s yiwet n tarrayt akken ma llan.

Nniɣ-d, nnig n tmental-a, tihawt-is deg twennaḍt terna-yas-d afud ameqqran acku tawennaḍt daɣen d tafelwit, d aɣebaz yesselmaden. Imdanen ur tt-frinen ara kan akka. Rran ɣur-s,

31 R.Kahlouche, 2002, La refrancisation des enseignes à Tizi-Ouzou : qu’on est-il depuis 1996 ?, In Passerelles, n°24, Numéro apparu sous le titre : Peuples, identités et langues berbères. Tamazight face à son avenir, Pp.127 -135.
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

fkan-as azal acku d tin s izemren ad d-segzin ayen i ten-iceɣben.

Tin ɣur-s, ad d-iniɣ, tura deg umaḍal, mi ara gen yimussnawen tizrawin ɣef tira neɣ mi ara ttmeslayen yimussnawen ɣef tira, ur ttɣiman ara kan deg unamek-is amezwaru, anda tira terza anagar ayen yellan d asnulfu (création) akka am tsekla, taɣamsa… Maca tura mi ara yili umeslay ɣef tira ttarran tamawt ɣer wayen akk yuran : journal intime, recettes, notices, les formulaires administratifs, listes des courses, mots laissés à un fils, à un ami, petites annonces, bulletin météo, SMS, atg.

Γef wannect-a amedya, H. Boyer yessemgared gar tira (écriture) akked d ujerred -ma nezmer ad as-nsemmi akka- (scription). Awal "tira" seqdacen-t i wayen yellan d asnulfu, ma d awal "ajerred" seqdacen-t i wayen ideg yenqes wazal n usnulfu, akka am : (Ti i d-uddreɣ iwsawen).

Ihi, d wasmi i d-yewwi ad nerr tamawt ɣer tira n tmaziɣt anda tebɣu tili acku akken i tura M. Rispail, deg udlis "Le francique" : "Dire qu’une langue existe, c’est déjà un peu participer à sa survie".

Nekni ma nura-tt, ma nga fell-as tizrawin, mačči d asider ara tt-nessider maca d asnerni ara tt-nesnerni, d asimɣer ara tt-nesimɣer gar tutlayin n umaḍal.

Ad d-rnuɣ kra n tmuɣliwin i wimi i ilaq ad nerr tamawt, ad nemmeslay fell-asent, ad nwelleh imdanen akken tamaziɣt ad taɣ ugar amḍiq-is deg tmetti :

- Yewwi-d ɣef yimdanen ad tt-sqedcen nnig n wannect-a acku ɣas, d tidet, aṭas i tt-yuran maca, deg tama-nniḍen, aṭas yimukan ideg ur d-ttbin ara. LLan wid i yessmenyifen ad arun taɛrabt, tarumit wala tamaziɣt. Ayen ɣef ara yesḥisef yiwen mačči kan anagar tira ; yella wayen i d-yekkan nnig-s, yesseqraḥ, yesserfay (ahat), yessewham, imi ula d ismawen i d-fernen kra n yimdanen i thunna-nsen, i yisensuyen-nsen, atg., ur sɛin ara akk assaɣ la d yidles-nneɣ, la d tutlayt-nneɣ, la d twennaḍt-nneɣ, la tmurt-nneɣ. Ad naf ismawen yecban :

- 130 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

aḥbab, ezzeytuna, el aḥlam, eliǧtihad, ennexla, el itihad, ennour, macaallah, rreḥma, titanic, azur, top, tic tac, zephir, le rapide, aigle, TGV, les amis, le faucon, hip hop, etc.

Γer tama-nsen ad naf wid i yefkan azal i tmaziɣt; uran s tmaziɣt, fernen-d ismawen i iwatan idles-is: awren, adrar, lbaz, talwit, timlilit, itri, tiziri…

Yuɣal d adabu, i ireglen zik tafat i tmaziɣt, i tt-yesseqdacen ugar wid yennuɣen fell-as. Ma nmuqel ad naf aṭas n tsuddwin n ddewla i yuran s tmaziɣt.

Ilmend n waya i d-yewwi fell-aɣ ad newwet amek ara d-ibin wazal-is s usemres-is deg yal amdiq.

ANSuf VISIEN TER LMAzib

# Ahilen d yidlisen iɣurbizen

# Tamuɣli n uselmad

Sadeq BENDALI

Mi ara nessiked $er wamek i iteddu uselmed n tutlayt tamazi$t, deg u$erbaz nne$, assa; nezmer ad d-nessukkes seg-s kra n usirem.

Tuget n yiselmaden d wid yettaken ul nsen deg umahil nsen aheggar. Assa$ yellan gar-asen akked tutlayt nsen am win n mmi-s $er tyemmat. Tamasit nsen meqqret. Amur ameqqran n yiselmaden d tselmadin teggen axeddim nsen s tayri yerna d nitni kan i d imezwura i iwatan, i yellan deg unnar n tidet.

Äeddan azal n 13 yiseggasen di termit, lec$al s ttawil kan iteddun.

Abrid i yu$ uselmed n tutlayt simmal yettseggim.

Tarselt ressan-tt yiselmaden n tsuffe$t n Mulud At Mâemmer (n 1995). Aseqqamu Unnig n Timmuz$a (H.C.A) d netta kan i ibedden $er tama nsen s drus n wallalen i yesâa. Yal aseggas ne$ sin, yessuddus-d timliliyin d tannanin n usile$.

Iselmaden-a, mazal amur ameqqran deg-sen, di twuri, xas akken uguren i ttmagaren maççi drus. Deg yiseggasen-a ineggura rennun-d $ur-sen at turagt i d-iteff$en lad$a, si tesdawiyin n Tizi Uzzu d Bgayet. Ddeqs n yineggura-a, tu$-iten d inelmaden n yimezwura mi llan deg u$erbaz alemmas.

Azrar n tsutwin yeqqen, irennu, yetti$zif.

Ma tella ta$ult i yesran i wussisen yal ass d tin n unadi ussnan. Yessefk ad nessifrer, ad nessizdeg, ad nessetrer ugar aselmed n Tmazi$t. Ma yella deg wayen yerzan tarrayt n uselmed, aselmad yesâa ansi yezmer ad d-yettagem, deg

- 132 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

wayen yeânan ugbiren utlayanen (ilugan n tutlayt : tajerrumt, taseddast, amawal) yessefk-as ahat ad ye$z iman-is ires ne$ anu s tallelt n yimeddukkal-is d wallalen nniven. Ineggura-a, d idlisen n tutlayt (xas drus i yellan) d yiwfusen i$urbizen i yesseéreg u$lif n usedwel a$elnaw, i yal aswir. Ha-t-a, d$a b$i$ ad d-fke$ tamu$li fell-asen, di sin yixfawen. Ad d-zwire$ seg yivrisen d yisental, imir-n ad zri$ $er yiferdisen n tutlayt d umawal umris. Di taggara, ad d-fke$ kra n yisumar i ttwali$ sâan azal i usemres.

# 1- Ivrisen d yisental

Ma nessukk tivt $er udlis n useggas alemmas amezwaru (1AM), ahat yeooa-t wakud. Ama deg yider ama di tal$a, ur yelli d allal axatar ara yernun afud i ulmud n unelmad. Deg useqdec n uwfus-a, nesmenyaf ad yettâawan uselmad inelmaden-is s yiwellihen. Isental i ttwali$ s wazal nsen, ad ten-naf deg yivrisen n t$uri : timecrevt n R. Äellic, sb 44; anekcum $er u$erbaz, sb 49 (ilaq ad yemmug di tazwara n useggas a$urbiz); yennayer, sb 75; imensi n yibeââac, sb 80; Favma n Sumer, sb 86; abazin, sb 98 (d asewwi aqbayli); tasaft n uwa$ezniw, sb 120. Yelha yerna ilaq ad yernu uselmad ivrisen nniven iwatan i yiswan u$ur yeb$a ad yessiwev, deg uselmed s tarrayt nni n tsegmisent n usenfar.

Awfus a$urbiz n useggas wis 2 "Adlis-iw n Tmazi$t" d yiwen wallal n ulmud i$er yezmer ad yettu$al unelmad yal tikkelt, ama deg uxxam (abeâda) ne$ di tne$rit, deg u$erbaz. Ivrisen i yegber, ttawin-d $ef tsekla tatlayt (timawit) d wansayen n Leqbayel, jebbden-d inelmaden d tnelmadin nne$, ssekcamen-ten-id deg yirebbi n t$erma nne$, leddin-asen allen d wulawen, $ef yigerrujen n yidles n ugdud nsen. Azal i tesâa tmacahut ta$erfant, nekkni nessen-it seg wasmi nella d "ileqqaqen". Tabrat i yellan deg wahil-a, d tagnit i yinelmaden akken ad ssenfalin $ef wufuren nsen, di tutlayt tayemmant (n tyemmat). S tira ad izmiren ad d-gelmen tawennavt ideg ttidiren. S uzray seg umeslay $er tira ara taf Tmazi$t amkan ger tutlayin nniven, azekka.

Deg uswir n useggas alemmas wis krad ara snernin yinelmaden timussniwin nsen $ef wullis amakun d uzenzi$ n Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 133 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

yimigan, d uglam n uwadem d wadeg, akked udiwenni mi ara d-yadef, di tmacahut. Ula d asegzi d tebrat yettwazerwen di sin yiswiren yezrin, u$alen-d deg wahil n useggas-a. Tabrat tamagnut, tedda-d yid-s tebrat tadeblant, asegzi yusa-d s telqey. Ayen igerrzen, deg usenfar-a aneggaru d agbar n yisental ussnanen. Ivrisen Anagraw n yiîij (sb 70), Amtiweg n umaval (sb 74), Ageffur (sb 79) d Waman (sb 83) mmalen belli Tamazi$t yebdan d tutlayt tulmidt tezmer war ugur ad tu$al d tutlayt n uselmed, awi-d kan ad as-tettunefk tegnit d wallalen.

Ma d ahil n useggas aneggaru n uselmed alemmas, yettawi-d deg usenfar amezwaru, $ef tullist tameéyant di te$zi n sviset (6) tgezmin. Asenfar wis sin igebren snat n tgezmin d asfukel. Deg uswir-a, igerrez ma nessekcem inelmaden di t$uri d tegzi d uzraw n tullisin. Ma yessiwev uselmad ad d-yeslal (ne$ ad d-yessekfel) tayri n tira nsent deg unelmad d$a d ayen yufraren mavi. Ahat, ad ilin wid ara ya$en abrid-a, deg yimal, ad u$alen d imura d ineggalen, ay$er ala !?

# Iferdisen n tutlayt d umawal umris

Iselmaden d yimaswaven n Tmazi$t i iveffren tannanin n usile$ $er umussnaw n tutlayt nne$ Naser Ayt Weâli, sâan zzher. Nessaram ad t-sâun akk wid i d-yeqqimen ne$ i d-irennun. Tajmilt-iw i Naser, meqqret, $ef wayen ixeddem i usnefli d usetrer n uselmed n tutlayt n Yuba wis sin. Yefka i uselmad amazi$ allal s wayes ara yessiwev ula d netta ad yefk allal i unelmad akken ad yelmed iman-is s tlelli yerna ad d-yekfel wayen yellan d tamussni, yeffer deg-s. Tasegmisent n usenfar lemden-tt yiselmaden n Tmazi$t uqbel wiyév yerna tebda la tetta$ aéar deg yi$erbazen, inelmaden u$en yid-s tanumi, u$alen êemmlen aîas ad $ren Tamazi$t.

Zware$-d awal $ef ulmud n tutlayt i iteddun cwiî cwiî, maca ilaq-as llsas iseêêan, maççi d kra. Taki d tameslayt nne$, maççi d urar kan ! Ur yessefk ara ad néerr tuccva ad as-neqqar, "maâlic" ne$ "ulac u$ilif", aya d ayen ur nesâi azal. Ur iwulem ara ad nesselmed tal$iwin n wawalen i yeff$en i yilugan ussnanen n tutlayt ne$ ad d-nesnulfuy ayen yellan, yakan.
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Mi zerwe$ ugbiren n yiwfusen i$urbizen ufi$ aîas n yimedyaten n wayen yeêwaoen ase$ti:

- Amatar udmawan wis 3 n wasuf amalay: nettaf-it, tikkelt d "i", tikkelt tayev d "ye" akked "y", anamek-is akken i ak-yehwa taruv, ur ilaq ara ad kemmlen yiselmaden akka acku tutlayt tesâa "isuvaf" akken yeb$u yili! Yessefk i yiselmaden d yimaswaven ad âiwden tamu$li deg waya. Ha-t-a wamek yella ulugen:
- Amatar udmawan wis 3 n wasuf amalay (netta): yettili d "i" ma yella sdat yiwet n tergalt (ibedd, igezzem, irennu, imuqel). Yettili d "ye" ma yella sdat snat tergalin -ama mgaradent ama d tussda- (yettbedda, yeéra, yegzem, yerna, yeéra) da, lemmer ad d-nini "iéra" waki d isem, aknaw-is "id$a$en" maççi d amyag.
- Asegzan (avris, sb 74 -1AM) - imsegzi (ad cfu$ sb 53 - 3AM): imyagen sselwi, sse$ti, ssexsi, sâan yiwet n tal$a d umyag ssegzi; imi ismawen n tigawt i d-yeff$en seg-sen d aselway, ase$tay, asexsay s "ay" di taggara, yessefk win d-yessegzayen ad yili $ef yiwet n tal$a, ad as-nini asegzay - avris asegzay s tmerna n ay di taggara ula d netta.
- Agaz: sli$ i ufakul i d-yennan awal yekka-d si Ttergit maca ula d taneqqivt d awal yellan di Teqbaylit (ay$er ara yettwakkes kan akka?) Tamazi$t-aki d ayen ibanen maççi akka ara teqqim - ad teddu $er sdat, teêwao aseb$er ugar mi ara tekcem deg waîas n ta$ulin. Ahat, ma iwata, ad yettusemmi "agaz" i lgaz imi awal-a lgaz ur nettumaze$ ara izewwir s "l" amagrad n tutlayt nniven (Tafransist ne$ Taârabt).
- Tamsertit "n+u", sb 103 – 2AM: yessefk ad tettwakkes acku ur tezmir ara ad tili temsertit ger tenze$t n d te$ri. Tettili temsertit mi ara mlilen sin yimesla ibeddel ususru.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 135 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

- Tamsirt "urmir ibaw" ne$ "urmir ibaway", sb 92 - 2AM + sb 74 -5AF: yessefk ad tettwakkes, ad d-yili use$ti n wugul, ad ternu kan tamawt $er temsirin n tal$a tibawt, anda ara yessegzi uselmad i yinelmaden-is belli "urmir d wanav ur sâin ara tal$a tibawt d anav ussid d wurmir ussid i asen-irevvlen tal$a tibawt".
- Tumyigt - tarumyigt (tafyirt), sb 31d 53 - 3AM + sb 53 - 4AM: Mi ara teérev tal$a n "umyig - tumyigt" tettemcabi $er tin n yirbiben unciw, ucmit, uzwi$ i d-yekkan seg yimyagen ncew, cmet, izwi$ tettban-d am wakken tekka-d ula d nettat seg umyag, maca tekka-d seg yisem "amyag" yerna deg umawal amazi$ ulac amyag "myeg". Si tama nniven, ilaq ad nwali belli yettili usuddem seg yisem s tmerna n udfir "an" (éer amawal n tmazi$t tatrart n ACB n Bgayet: amaz$an, amiran, anzeggan, a$erman). Irbiben ilan adfir "an" i d-yekkan seg yimyagen ggten d ayen kan: ahrawan, aberkan, a$ezzfan. Acu$er ihi ur nesmenyaf ara ad nesseqdec tal$iwin-a: amyagan, aramyagan (tafyirt tamyagant - taramyagant)? Tiki llant-d s tmerna n udfir "an" i "amyag" d tmerna n uzwir n tibawt "ar".
- Tal$a n uttwa$ twa-twaker, sb 24 - 4AM: ilaq ad tt-yesse$ti yal aselmlad, ad tu$al akka: azwir d ttwa ara nrennu i umyag amenzu akken ad yu$al d attwa$ "Ttwaker, ttwakkes…".
- Tal$a nn-nneqlab, sb 24 - 4AM: tal$a-a maççi d attwa$ acku attwa$ yemmal tigawt iverrun $ef walbeâv bla ma yexdem-itt netta.
- Tal$a taêerfit (tamezwarut), sb 24, 33 d 44 - ad cfu$ - 4AM: d tuccva ur nlaq ara ad tili deg wahil unsib. Ur iwulem ara ad nettu belli tal$a taêerfit, sâan-tt akk yimyagen ama d amenzu ama d asuddim. Qqaren-as s Tefransist "l’infinitif". I wakken ad nessemgired ger snat n tal$iwin, amyag amenzu ad as-neqqar "tal$a tamenzut n umyag" (md: yelmed), asuddim ad as-neqqar "tal$a tasuddimt n umyag" (md: yesselmed).

Ma nu$al-d $er tal$a taêerfit, tin n umedya 1ᵘ d - 136 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

"lmed", tin n umedya wis 2 d "sselmed". Ha-tt-a tbadut : tal$a taêerfit d tal$a n umyag uqbel ad yefti, d nettat i d tameéyant ger tal$iwin n umyag, ur tesâi ara amatar udmawan.

- Asnubget ne$ tinnubga, sb 57 - ad cfu$ - 2AM +36 d 41 - 5AF ?! sin wawalen mgaraden ur sâin ara yiwen n unamek : asnubget d leârava ne$ d ancad ma d anubget d tirza n yinebgi $er win i t-iâerven. Ihi, avris s wayes ara d-tâervev "d asnubget".
- Asenked ne$ tanekda ?! : Ula da, yif-it ad smersen yiselmaden awal "asenked".
- Izri ibaway ne$ izri ibaw ?! : inelmaden ara ye$ren Tamazi$t, di 5Af ad lemden izri ibaway (éer asebter 66); mi wwven $er u$erbaz alemmas ad ibeddel ad yu$al d izri ibaw (éer sb 57 - 1AM, éer sb 36 - 2AM). Deg yiswiren nniven da$en, ad d-u$alen alamma d ibaway d yilaway nni (éer sb 63 - 3AM, tafelwit n tseftit n usebter 86 - 4AM).

# 3- Kra n yisumar i usemres

Ma ssurfen-iyi yimeddukkal iselmaden d yimaswaven, ad d-ssnekde$ kra n yisumar i tt$illi$ zemren ad rnun kra n ufud deg uselmed d ulmud imi sâan assa$ d wugbiren n tutlayt, ha-ten-aya :

Tal$a n wurmir ussid d wanav ussid i d-yettilin s "ay" ne$ "uy" di taggara n umyag, ad ternu kan $er tal$a n temlellit, deg yiswiren akk. Ad sseqdacen yiselmaden d yinelmaden nsen s tlelli, sin wawalen i ilan yiwen n unamek "ticcert" d "tefrayt".

Ad sseqdacen yiselmaden d yinelmaden nsen s tlelli, sin wawalen i ilan yiwen n unamek "tizdit" d "tjerrivt n tuqqna" ma d ajerriv n tuqqna ad yettwakkes. Ad yeqqim kan "ajerriv", netta $ezzif $ef tjerrivt. Yezmer da$en ad yesseqdac uselmad "tajerrivt" mi ara d-yili umeslay $ef tinna i nettaf di tazwara n tseddart ne$ ma ur tcudd ara sin yiferdisen.

Ad as-nsemmi i twuri n umatar udmawan deg umyag attwa$ d umyag n t$ara "ubdir", ma d asemmad-is, ad yili d asemmad Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 137 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

n wubdir imi ur d-yemmal ara win igan tigawt : yeçça uqcic ifires. (ye d amatar udmawan, "uqcic" d asemmad n umigaw - yemmeçç yifires (da, ye d amatar udmawan, d ubdir ma d "yifires" d asemmad n wubdir).

Asemmad agucclan yezmer ad yili d asemmad n yisem ma yegguccel isem (md : tamurt n Umazi$), ma yegguccel amernu d asemmad n umernu (md : Sâan drus n yidrimen).

Isemmaden igucclanen d wi : n yisem, n umernu, n umvan, n urbib, n umqim.

Ad neg isem amatar n uma$un i umatar di tal$a n uma$un (md : yuran : y ----- n d amatar n uma$un, ura d afeggag).

Ad nessawal i tewsit n tefyirt tamattart, tafyirt tasestant (tasestant yekka-d seg umyag yettwassnen ssesten i yellan di Teméabt).

Ad nessawal asestan, isestanen i umattar, imattaren.

Llan sin waddaden : ilelli d umaruz. S umata, isem ma yella deg waddad amaruz yettbeddil maca llant tegnatin anda ur yettbeddil ara. (Tzemrem ad tafem asegzi alqayan deg "uwfus amaynut n tutlayt tamazi$t", isebtar 25 ar 28).

# Tasekla tagraɣlant :

# deg yiɣerbazen n tsekla

Djamel HAMRI

# a- A$erbaz Aklasiki (classicism):

Taklasikit seg zik i teîîef amviq aâlayen di seg tsekla, deg udem n tmu$li n tfelsafit, akken tella yi$erbazen iqburen n tmedyazt… deg udem n tikli, anamek-is yekcem deg yizuran iqburen i d-yiwarten si tsekla tayunanit taqburt.

Awal n teklasikit deg uzar yefruri-d seg wawal "classic", deg unamek-is di tsekla, d aferdis di tigriwin, tu$al sexdamen-tt d aferdis n tusna.

Tlul-d teklasikit di lber n Uruba, mbaâd mi-d tebda acrured tusna i d-yebnan di lqern wis xemseîîac (15), nezmer ad n-tebbet d asmi te$li "Qusîunîin" deg useggas n 1453 $ef yifassen n yiîerkiyen s ufus n Muêend Elfateê, deg yimiren suklen imusnawen d yimyura n Qusîunîin (Bizenîa), nutni glan yid-sen ayen akk uran s tlaîinit taqburt $er tmurt n Ïelyan d tmura i s-d-yezzin, maca Ïelyan tella d dduê n tsekla taklasikit, tenfufed $er tmurt n Fransa, anida tufa leb$i-s aîas i unerni, almi i yerran iman-nsen yirumyen d yiwriten n tidet n "Alika" d yiwet tama i d-yezgan di temdint n Atina, tamana$t n Lyunan.

Dayen ibedden, yefkan tigejda muqqren di tsekla tayunanit… d "Aristun", afeylasuf ameqqran, ma qrib ayen i d-yefka Aristun i teklasikit, yegga-yas tamendawt, degmi, yemmeslay-d aîas deg wudlis (Tamedyazt) $ef tzuri n temliliyin timedyazin d drama, maca yefka azal meqqren i Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 139 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

drama, deg-s Trajidi, kumidi akter $ef tzuri n temliliyin timedyazin qbel ayen nniven.

Di tallit-nni $ur-sen deg yimenza yuéen $er tmedyazt n ccna $er Iyunan d Öuman, amedya "Bulu" amedyaz afernan arumi aklasiki, akken di$en llan wid yuéen di tzuri n temliliyin timedyazin $er Iyunaniyen, amedya "Runsari".

Di lqern wis sbeâîac, imyura n Fransa ur d-cliâen di tmedyazt n ccna, maca iruê leb$i-nsen akter $er tmella$t di drama, trajidi, yella $ef iqerra n yiklasikiyen, win i d-yessulin tasekla n umezgun wagi d "Mulir" (1683), "Kurnayel" (1684) d "Rasin" (1699).

Ma d "Rasin yella d netta i d-yufraren di tqacuct n yiklasikiyen di lber n uruba, akken yella "Cikesbyir" yella $ef tqacuct n trumanisit, akken i yellan imedyazen-a deg yiwen n wakud, di lqern wis sbaâîac, imi d lqern ideg i d-tufrar tsekla s wudem muqqren, nezmer ad ner lewhi-nne$ aîas $er tem$er n ccan n "Rasin" di tmusni-s seg wayen i d-yuoew $er ufaylasuf afransi "Dikart", bab n wawal : (Nekk la ttxemmime$, ihi nekk lli$), nezmer ad d-nini "Rasin", têuza-t tawla n tfelsafit n "Dikart", imi yemmut deg useggas n 1650, waqbel-is s wezgen n lqern, dakken tafelsafit n "Dikart" ne$ tadikartit teîîef amviq muqqren deg walla$en n yimyura n Fransa, tefka-d di$en udem di teklasikit, dakken s uxemmem, alla$, loehd n tfekka d wegbur fiêel asugnen ne$ tazzla deffir n yiêulfan, begnen-d yimyura n Fransa di tallit n "Rasin" udem n trajidi d kumidi (lêif d tlufa i ten-yu$en) $er iyunaniyen i wakken ad as-ssiwven akk ayen tuêwao teklasikit seg udmawen tettawi, bedden-d deg udem n tudert n yigeldan d leêwaci-s.

Di lqern wis tmenîac 18, nger tamawt dakken imyura n Fransa bdan ttruéun ibubdar tamenwalit di tsekla taklasikit, ur êrisen ara $ef tlufa (trajidi) akken ad d-tili tcudd $er tudert n yigeldan weêd-s, akken di$en ur êrisen ara deg unecraê n (kumidi) akken ad tu$al d astewtew deg wayen ur nemâin, maca uéen akter $er tmenwalit, akter di tsugnent n tudert, ur telli ara tudert $ur-sen d tiwu$a yal ass, wala d tavsa ur nemâin.

- 140 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

£ef lewhi n tikli-nsen, uran (Drama n tilawt), nettat ur telli d tin yesruyen, ad yeqber umdan $er daxel si leêzen, fiêel ma crurqent-d wallen seg yimeîîi, akken di$en uran (Kumidi marifudi), icudd $er umeskar-is d "Marifu" nettat d tin yessawalen $er wucmumeê si daxel fiêel aqehqah-nni n waîas, s tidet tedda d tudert n yimiren di Fransa.

Di tallit ideg yebda îîrav n Fransa(1789) di taggara n lqern wis tmenîac 18, tebda tettnerni tsekla taklasikit, $ef wakken tella di tizwar, imi ad naf annag "Astiqrati" d annag n yigeldan d leêwac-is, teffer $ef tudert, imi i$um-d fell-as wannag aburowazi, yeb$a ad d-ibeggen annag-agi deg umezgun aklasiki deg uguren i d-yettemlil, $ef waya i d-tlul drama taburowazit $er tama n drama taklasikit.

Iban-d deg ubrid-agi amaynut umusnaw "Didar", maca ur yerri ara lewhi-s s drama taburowazit $er wayen tettidir deg uguren yettidir wumdan, deg udem dakken d amdan deg yiman-is, am tayri, karuh, tismin. Maca yerra lewhi-s $er tifin n tifrat s wudem, dakken d amdan ne$ d abruy di tmetti, d ucudu yellan gar-asen, drama taburowazit ur terri lmil-is $er wemdan dakken d amdan, maca netta d aselmad, d amejjay, d amezzenzu, d afellaê.

D win icudden $er tmetti, $ef waya amezgun aklasiki di Fransa yettim$ur, bdan ad d-tlalen i$erbazen d wudmawen i t-irefden, yettazzalen deffir n iêulfu n tudert iteddun $er zdat.

Gar wayen i d-yufraren di tgemmi n tsekla taqburt, deg wayen i$ef rran lmurud-nsen iklasikiyen, d tixutert n tutlayt $ef wayen tebna di tefses d tfelsafit, mexlaf irumansiyen yettarran lmil aîas $er usugnen, azamal d usufe$ n wayen ized$en daxel-nsen, akken tsenned teklasikit $ef walla$ ééayen yettmeyyizen s uxemmem, maççi taklasikit ur tt-yezdi$ ara wafra, maca anamek-is d asdukel gar uxemmem, asugnen d uêulfu deg yiwet n tmu$li yeççuren, $ef waya nnan "Rasin" aklasiki yella d win yufraren s waîas deg usugnen iêulfan n tayri, $ef wayen tettwassen teklasikit deg uxemmem i$emqen.

Ma akken llan iyunaniyen ur ooin kra ara yerren lbal di tsekla n tullizin, wama ooan-d aîas n tmezgunin, $ef waya ara nefhem iklasikiyen fkan azal i umezgun $ef tzuri nniven.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 141 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Ayen i$ef yers lewhi di tklasikit $ef tiyav, yessed $ef wejbad n yiman-is $er usentel, akud d wemkan, deg win semman ifennanen di krav n iferdisen, imcuden-agi i tcudd teklasikit tettwaddem-d di$en $er "Aristu" imi yerra-d lewhi $ur-s deg umkan d wakud di rray-is d imkemlen i lebni n walla$, bexlaf amezgun arumanisi $ef win ara d-nemmeslay, ur yeksib ara icuduyen-agi.

# Ad yikemmel :

- b- A$erbaz arumanisi (Romanticism)
- c- A$erbaz n tilawt (Réalism)
- d-A$erbaz azamal (Symbolism)

- 142 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Akkin i tefyirt neɣ Tajerrumt n uḍris

# Ilugan n uzeṭṭa n uḍris

Yahia BELLIL

Aḍris mačči kan d azrar n tefyar, ta deffir ta; d azeṭṭa yeddan i lmendad n yilugan yeflen akkin i tjerrumt n tefyirt. Ilugan-nni qqaren-asen tajerrumt n uḍris. Aḍris, ma tewqem tira-s, ila azenziɣ amatu. Deg-s ttilint kra n tgezmin, anamek-nsent ittekk-d seg unamek-is amatu. Ma nerfed-d tigezmin-a yal yiwet iman-is, yezmer ad yejlu fell-asent unamek, neɣ ad qqiment d timenneqsa. Acku d azeṭṭa i asent- yettaken anamek ummid. Ɣef waya i ilaq ad teddu tira i lmend n yilugan n uzeṭṭa n uḍris.

Tazrawt-a ad tili d tiririt ɣef kra n tuttriwin am:

- Amek i yettili unebḍi n yisalan deg uḍris?
- Amek i iteddu uḍris, seg tefyirt ɣer tayeḍ, akken ad yesdukel isalan imaynuten d yiferdisen yettwassnen yakan?

# 1- Asentel d yisali

S umata, tafyirt tettwaslaḍ s krad n yiberdan:

- tafyirt d inaw ilan anmek (Yeswa umcic ayefki. / Yeswa umcic isɣaren. - ?-);
- tafyirt d agraw n wawalen ideg qqnen yisemmaden ɣer useɣru s wassaɣen n tseddast (Chomsky);
- tafyirt d inaw yezdin isali akked usentel.

Tasleṭ s ubrid-a aneggaru, ad as-nsemmi tamuɣli tawurant. D tamuɣli-a ara neṭṭef d tasalelt, ad nessebded fell-as awal ɣef uzeṭṭa n uḍris.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 143 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Deg tmuɣli-a tawurant, llan sin n wuguren :

- Tafyirt teṭṭafar tiɣessiwin n tseddast ; maca, amek ara yefrez deg-s wayen yellan d amaynut ɣef uqdim ?
- Amek ara aɣent snat n taggayin n wawalen, deg tefyirt, snat n tewsatin n yisalan : aqbur d umaynut ?

S umata, deg tefyirt, ttilin sin n yiferdisen addayen :

- Amezwaru d ayen yettwassnen (neɣ xersum d ayen yenneḥsaben yettwassen, iban) ara yilin d tasalelt i umsiwel.

Aferdis-a ad as-nsemmi ASENTEL.

- Wis-sin d ayen ara d-yini umsiwel ɣef usentel ; d ayen ara yilin d amaynut. Ad as-nsemmi ISALI.

Md :

Jeddi Mangellat

Jeddi Mangellat d aṣeḥbi. Iruḥ-d si tmurt n ccerq, aṭas aya. Di lxaṭer-is, ad yesken tafat i wulawen tt-ixuṣṣen.

[Henri Genevois, Monographies villageoises, sb 164, Edisud]

Deg tseddart-a ad aɣ-banent tɣawsiwin-a i snat. Ma netter :

- Anwa i ɣef nettmeslay ?
- Ɣef Jeddi Mangellat. (Tiririt tban).

Ihi, ayen yettwassnen, yefka-t-id uzwel, d Jeddi Mangellat i yeṭṭfen amkan d asentel deg tefyirt tamezwarut akked tid i d-iḍefren ama s wudem n yisem s timmad-is ama s win n umatar udmawan (I, ye) neɣ n umqim (is).

Ma d ayen i yerzan asentel neɣ ayen i d-nenna fella-s, yettuneḥsab d isali, neɣ ayen i d-yellan d amaynut ; ayen yellan ur t-nessin ara yakan ɣef Jeddi Mangellat, nuɣal tura nessen-it : d acu-t ? ansa i d-yusa ? melmi ? d acu i d asenfar-is?

# 1.1- Awan n tmuɣli tawurant

Tasleḍt tawurant tferrez gar tɣessiwin n tefyar i yemgarrden,

- 144 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

deg tilawt, tettwali-tent tjerrumt n tefyirt mgadant.

Amedya : - Ad yili ugeffur, azekka. (neɣ ) - Azekka, ad yili ugeffur.

Gar tefyar-a, tasleḍt tamagnut ur tettwali ara kra n umgirred.

"Azekka" d asemmad n wakkud ; yezwar neɣ yeggra, kif kif.

Ma d tamuɣli tawurant ad taf yella umgirred imi asezwer d uwexxer n wawal "azekka" ibeddel anebḍi n yisalan deg tefyar-a.

D tidet, deg tinawt, snat n tefyar-a ad kecment deg snat n tegnatin yemgarrden, imi :

- tamezwarut tezmer ad tili d tiririt ɣef tuttra : "Melmi ara yili ugeffur ? " D acu ara d-yeḍrun (ara d-yilin)
- tis-snat ad d-terr ɣef : "azekka ?"

S waya, ad negzu taɣawsa :

- deg tefyirt tamezwarut, "azekka" yewwi-d aferdis amaynut ; ihi d isali ;
- deg tayeḍ, "azekka" d aferdis yettwassnen yakan deg tefyirt ; ihi d asentel.

Tamuɣli tawurant ur d-tecqi ara d tɣessa n tefyirt s wudem n tseddast ; annar-is d taɣessa tisalit. Teskan-d amek i yeddes deg tefyirt unebḍi n yisalan d wamek i yettikki kra n yisger deg tneflit n teywalt.

Am wakken diɣen, deg tefyirt, yettili :

- usentel agejdan (N) : Muḥend-nneɣ d afeḥli.
- yisali agejdan (L)  : Muḥend-nneɣ d afeḥli.
- yisali amuran (LM) : Imdanen i yuɣalen ass-a d imerkantiyen llan zik d imelluẓa.
- uzarug (Z)          : Imdanen i yuɣalen ass-a d a imerkantiyen llan zik d imelluẓa.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 145 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Azarug d awal i iteqqnen isali ɣer usentel ; yettili d amyag neɣ d tazelɣa n tilawt ur newwiḍ s timmad-is d isali. Di teggti, iteddu akked taggayt n yisali.

# 1.2 - Taneflit n yisali d usentel

Tuqqna n tigawt neɣ n tefyirt ɣer tin i tt-yezwaren yettili-d s kra n yiberdan am :

# 1.2.1- tuqqna s yimezdiyen

|Md :|Nefka-yas duru, yessusem.| | | | |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|Ne|fka -yas duru, ye ssusem| | | | |
|N1|Z|L1|L2|N2|L3|
|Nefka-yas duru, dɣa yessusem| | | | | |

# 1.2.2- tuqqna ɣer yiferdisen igejdanen

Md : Imdanen i yuɣalen ass-a d imerkantiyen llan zik d imelluẓa.

Anwa gar yisumar-a i nezmer ad t-nernu i tefyirt-a ?

- a- Ur ttwalin ara ameɣbun.
- b- Tura, imi rwan, uɣalen ur ṭṭallayen ara ɣer umeɣbun.
- c- Rwan ccer d usemmiḍ.
- d- Ur nwin ara ad d-yaweḍ wass ad rwun aɣrum.
- e- Ugaren fell-asen yidrimen.

Ticki teqqen tefyirt tis-snat ɣer tefyirt tamassaɣt neɣ ɣer kra n uferdis ur yellin d agejdan, ur d-yettawi ara uzrar n tefyar anamek ummid. Yettas-d uneggaru-a ur iwulem ara i tegnit, d amenneqsu.

Asečči n tefyirt i tayeḍ ilaq ad d-yettili kan ɣef usentel agejdan neɣ ɣef yisali agejdan, mačči ɣef yiḥricen-nniḍen n tefyirt.

S lmendad n waya, ad naf b, c, d sefken i tegnit ; a, e ur laqen ara, imi timerna qqnent ɣer yiḥricen ur nebdid s yiman-nsen - dagi d tamassaɣt :

- 146 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Imdanen i yuɣalen ass-a d imerkantiyen llan zik d imelluẓa.

# 2- Azeṭṭa n uḍris

Llan 4 n yilugan n uzeṭṭa n uḍris³². Ha-ten aya :

# 2.1- Alugen n usmekti

Akken ad yili uḍris yezḍa, ilaq ad d-ttuɣalen, deg tnefli-ines seg tefyirt ɣer tayeḍ, yiferdisen ara d-yesmektayen isental yezrin. Seg tefyirt ɣer tayeḍ, isalan ad bedden ɣef yiferdisen ara d-yettuɣalen (yisental). Neɣ, yal tafyirt tamaynut ad tessebded isali-ines ɣef yiwen n uferdis agejdan n tefyirt yezrin, ara terr d asentel-ines.

Alugen-a yerza isental n tefyar. Deg uḍris, tarusi n yiwen n uzrar n wawalen n usmekti, i yessedduyen tifyar ɣer zdat, yessefk ad tessifses ɣef unermas tukza n yisental d yisalan. Ma nmuqel kra n uḍris n tmaziɣt, akken ad nwali amek i d-yettili usmekti n yisental, ad naf tutlayt-a tla krad n wallalen iteqqnen tigezmin ta ɣer ta.

# 2.1.1- Asmekti s umatar d umqim udmawan

Amatar udmawan :

S umata, asmekti n usentel itekkay ɣef umatar udmawan i yettawi umyag n usumer neɣ n tefyirt yernan ɣer yidis n tayeḍ.

Md 1 : Yemlal Muḥa, iḍelli, yiwen n uqcic n Tefrit iɣef ur d-zgint ara wallen-is mraw n yiseggasen aya […] Yeẓra-t kan yaɛqel-it.

Md 2 : Faḍma teḥjeb ur teḥjib. Anebdu d tefsut s lekmal, ideg ara yettqeggil baba-s ɣer tfellaḥt, nettat yid-s, ama testaɛmil.

32 CHAROLLES Michel, deg tesɣunt LANGUE FRANCAISE, uṭṭun 38 n useggas 1978.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 147 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

tessway tibḥirt, ama tetturar, tettabaɛ ifrax.

[Les cahiers de Belaid, 33]

# Amqim udmawan :

Asmekti s umqim d yiwen wallal i yeskanen amek ara yettuɣal umqim deg umkan n usentel. Amqim yettili d ilelli, yettili d awsil.

# a- Ma d ilelli :

- # Amqim udmawan :

Md 1: Nek d Maɛṭub aṭas aya ideg nemyussan […] Aṭas i aɣ-icerken […] Di tazwara, d tanudda-w. Tis-snat, tudrin-nneɣ mqarabent ; tis-tlata, akken i neɣra di lakul alammi d aswir wis 6. Syin akkin, netta ikemmel di llisi n Bni Dwala, nekkini kecmeɣ ɣer llisi n Faḍma n Sumer […]

Asmi meqqrit, ruḥ a zzman, uɣal-d a zzman, nemlal-d deg umḍiq n ccna. Netta yekkat ɣef Tmaziɣt, nekkini kif-kif.

[Malika Domran, Actualités et Culture Berbères]
- # Md2 :

Jean akked Ṭawes suffɣen-d, netta isefra s tefransist akked tterjima n yisefra s teqbaylit, nettat yiwen n wungal isem-is "Jacinthe noire".

[Awal ɣef Dda Lmulud, 50]
- # Md3 :

Kullas nekk ttruɣ fell-as

Ma d netta yezha wul-is

Aql-i am win yettewten s rrsas

Ma sliɣ wi d-yuddern isem-is

[Sliman Azem, Aḥbib n wul-iw]

Md : Muqel anwa ara tawiḍ deg yidlisen-a. Wa n tsekla n teqbaylit, wagi-nniḍen n umezruy n Tmazɣa.

# - Amqim n wayla :

Md : Ha-t udlis n Racid ma ad t-tawiḍ, maca d aylaw i yelhan.

[Si Muḥend]

- Yenneɣna Bakli ; yeddrem uxxam-is, yuɣal d axrib.
