# 2.1.2- Tasbadut

Tasbadut d allal n usmekti n kra n yisem s timmad-is. Tettili-d s tmerna n urbib ameskan.

Md 1 : Yella yiwen di Tewrirt, qqaren-as Ɛli Iɛekkucen. Yella yesɛa tlata n watmaten-is : di rebɛa yid-sen. Ulakkayen, Iɛekkucen-agi d at ddreɛ, d at nnif.

[Henri Genevois, Monographies villageoises, sb 221, Edisud]

Md 2 : Nteddu almi newweḍ ɣer yiwen n uxxam, yeṭṭurfa cwiṭ ɣef taddart. Nufa dinna yiwet n temɣart tberri ibawen ; tefreḥ d aya yis-neɣ. Nečča ɣur-s imensi, neswa lqahwa, nekker ad nejbu. Dɣa tessawel i yiwen n umusebbel yedda yid-neɣ almi nfel akkin i udrar, metwal Igawawen. Deg uxxam-nni i nga, mi d-yezzi useggas, di 56, Agraw n Sumam, deg Uzellagen.
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

# Md 3 : Asmi tefra, kecmeɣ-tt d aselmad ɣer uɣerbaz Oscar di Tewrirt.

Aɣerbaz-a yuɣal tura d axxam n cambiṭ n taddart.

# 2.1.3. Tikkesrert s wawal

Aya yerza asemres n kra n wawal ur d-nettwabder ara deg tefyar yezrin. Ad yili d asentel ara d-yesmektin ayen yettwassnen yakan :

# Md 1 : Yiwen n wass, mcawaren At-Wasif d At-Yanni, nnan-as i lḥaǧ Arezqi At-Meɛtuq :

- Ad-nettixer i ssuq-agi : ad newqem ssuq deg wakal-nneɣ !
- Yenna-yasen :
- - Yirbeḥ : ad nettixer i At-Uqbil.

Lameɛna, nnan-as :
- - Ccerṭ, ad newqem ssuq n lǧemɛa di tasift n lḥedd deg wakal n At-Wasif.

Yenna-yasen :

[Henri Genevois, Monographies villageoises, sb 221, Edisud]

# Md 2 : Sidi Lmeḥfuḍ yenɣa yiwen n urgaz di ssuq, s ujenwi.

Tawaɣit-a ad d-teglu s tiyaḍ. Ɣas d amrabeḍ, tamgerṭ tessawal i ttar.

Dagi, taggayt n yisem "tawaɣit-a" d "temgerṭ" qqnent ɣer umyag "yenɣa". Ɣef waya, asezwer n usenfal ur d-yegli s kra n yisali amaynut; yella-d kan d asmekti n wayen yezwaren.

# Asmekti yettili-d s yiferdis neɣ s umatu :

# Md1: Axxam n Bakli yebna s udɣaɣ d texmirt; tiɛrestin ulint s lyajur d lǧir, ssqef d igisem d uqermud n legniz.

# Md 2 : Amɣar iferres, mmi-s icerru, tilawin leqqḍent, arrac ttḥawacen. Tawacult akk txeddem.

[Ɛmer Mezdad, Iḍ d wass, 121]

# 2.2- Alugen n tfara

Akken ad yili uḍris yezḍa, ilaq ad d-teglu tneflit-is s yisalan imaynuten yeddan d usentel. Yessefk ad yaẓ ɣer zdat, ur itezzi ara kan ɣef yiwen n yisali.

Afir am wa : "Leḥbab-nni n zik kfan"

[Sliman Azem, Tura jerbeɣ]

Ma nkemmel-as akka :

Leḥbab-nni n zik kfan

Ulac win i d-yeggran

Mmuten akk fnan

Ad naf tinawt (neɣ asefru) yeffeɣ i ulugen n tfara. Ulac kra n umaynut deg yefyar i d-irnan ; tezzin tennḍen.

Ladɣa, ilaq yal tafyirt ad d-tawi, ma drus maḍi, yiwen n uferdis amaynut.

Md : Cennuɣ ɣef tmurt ; tamurt n baba d jeddi.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 151 -

# 2.2.1- Tafara s yiwen usentel:

|N1|L1|

|N1|L3|

(N : asentel / L : isali)

Md 1 : Qqaren yella yiwen n umeksa ikess tajlibt-is di sseḥra.

Mkul tameddit, qbel ad iṭṭes, ad d-yini Lmursel. Netta ad d-ittawi taqsiṭ, ssur ad itezzi i tejlibt ; mi tfuk teqsiṭ, ssur idewwer, yemdel. Yiwen n yiḍ, ameksa yewwi-t yiḍes qbel ad tt-ifuk.

[PKA, 376]

Da, asentel "ameksa" yettuɣal-d deg yal tafyirt.

Md2 : Narsis yeglef seg tikli. Yaweḍ ɣer yiwet n tala, yekcem ad isew. Yeddummeɣ kan ɣer umdun, iwala udem-is deg waman-nni imẓerrfen.

Amatar n wudem wis kraḍ d uwsil-is smektayen-d Narsis.

# 2.2.3- Tafara s yisental uddimen

Tafara-a tla sin n yiberdan.

# 2.2.3.1- Abrid amezwaru

Asentel amatu ad yili yettwwabder-d di tinawt. Yettefruri ɣef waṭas n yisental-iḍen. Tafara-a tettili s teggti deg usfukel d usegzi akked tgelma. Deg uḍris agelman, imuren n tɣawsa yettwagelmen ttaṭṭafen tasga n yisental n tefyar.

# Md

Tazeqqa n Tḥemmut tebna ɣef lqaɛa. Agens yessa, d azedgan. Leḥyuḍ lebbsen s tumlilt. Lemdawed qban yakk. Addaynin yuɣal d taxxamt.

[Ɛmer Mezdad, Iḍ d wass, 121]

Deg uḍris asegzan, amsiwel yettak-d aṭas n tmuɣliwin ɣef yiwen usentel.

# Md

# Azway n uzemmur

Teẓram, ahat, azway i tzewwim s uεekkaz cceṭṭ n tzemmurt, deg-s snat n txessarin: Tamezwarut, azhaḍ i tzehhḍem s umextaf, din ur tellu lewqama; kra n yisegmi.
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

yellan ad yarew deg useggas i d-iteddun ad yettuqseb, ad yerreẓ, ad yettwaclex.

Tis snat, tfehmem s kra n uεeqqa ara iḥaz umextaf ad yefxes ad yebḍu mnasef, ad d-yeqqim ala amegruc.

Wanag lukan txeddmem akken i d-nenna, yalli i d-yusa ccɣel n ucraw d llqeḍ yiwen, yeshel; yerna akka, lɣella ur tettḍaε ara: ad d-tettarram deg-s aṭas, tayeḍ ad d-tettas zeddiget, ur yettili deg-s la axeclaw wala akal.

[Boulifa, Méthode de… sb. 203-204]

# Asegzi:

# Tamuɣli n uselmad:

- azway ur yelhi ara (tikti) TILAWT
- azhaḍ iḍur tazemmurt d lɣella (analkam) AYEN IḌURREN
- acraw d ḥellu n tzemmurt, d tezdeg n nneɛma (asumer) AMEK I ILAQ

# 2.2.3.2- Abrid wis-sin:

Da, asentel amatu ur d-yettwader ara d awal s timmad-is deg tinawt / uḍris. D tigzi n wayen yeqqnen tafyirt ɣer tayeḍ i d tasarut n tifin n usentel amatu. Yezmer uḍris ad yili yeqqen s yimezdiyen n wadeg neɣ n wakud. Asezwer-nsen - am wakken d isemmaden ilelliyen yezwaren, s tmuɣli n tseddast - yeskan d acu-t usentel ideg d-frurin, ama d tarusi deg tallunt neɣ d tiddin deg wakud.

# Tarusi deg tallunt

Md: Netbaɛ-t armi ɣ-yessekcem ɣer texxamt… D lebḥer… Ɣef zelmeḍ mi ara tkecmeḍ, deg wammas d asawen, lḥiḍ yebna s urelluc, yefka tamuɣli ɣer tebḥirt… D lǧennet: tičintin, tilimtin, ijeǧǧigen, tiftilin di yal tiɣmert. Ar akessar maḍi, seddaw teɛrict, yiwen n udernu n lyasmin la d-iṭeggir rriḥa armi d axxam. Zdat-s, sin n yikersiwen n ssiman qublen ṭṭabla n rrxem.

[Said Sadi, Askuti, 83]

- 154 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Tiddin deg wakud

Md : Ɣef userwet

Aseggas-a d amerbuḥ ; teswa akken yelzem […] Lweqt n tmegra, jebbden, qqaren ahda am win yettqeddimen di lɣaba… Mi tekfa tmegra d umerres, ad tt-cudden d iquttyan, ad tt-neqqlen ɣer unnar, ad tt-sersen d taffa. Mi yenǧer, iḍerra unnar […] Ass deg ara srewten, ad awin leḥwal akk ilezmen […] Ɣer lǧiha n setta akka, ad ɛeddin ad gren ddersa [...] Imiren ad kkren ad qqnen, ad bdun arwa.

[Boulifa, Méthode 2ème année, 365]

# 2.2.4. Alugen n war tanmegla

Akken ad yili uḍris yezḍa, ur ilaq ara ad d-iban, deg tneflit-ines, kra n ukettur ara yilin mgal ayen i d-yettwabedren yakan, ama d awal s timmad-is, ama d tikti tuffirt. Tezmer tenmegla ad d-tban deg sin n yiswiren :

# Tanmegla timinawt :

Md1 : a- Yuba iruḥ iman-is ɣer udrar.

b- Yuba iruḥ ɣer udrar.

c- Yerkeb ɣef uɣyul n jeddi-s

d- Yessedda-t jeddi-s d yiwen n umeksa.

Tafyirt a tezmer ad teqbel akemmel s tefyirt c. Ma nerna ɣer-s tafyirt d ad d-tban tenmegla imi taggayt "iman-is" ur tqebbel ara ad tennulfu tekti n uddukel akked kra n umdan-iḍen.

Tafyirt b ad teqbel c, d imi ulac kra n tenmegla ara d-yennulfun.

# Md 2 : Tamacahut n lekdeb ideg ur tekki tidet.

Tanmegla n tmussni n tilawt :

Md : Yenǧer Ḥemmu tisilet deg uẓebbuj, yerna-yas tifekkalin n tassaft.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 155 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Win i d-yennan aya, iban ur yessin ara ayen iɣef yettmeslay. Di tilawt, tisilet ur tli ara tifekkalin. Tifekkalin teddunt d uzaglu, rennunt ɣef yimegraḍ n yizgaren mi ara kerrzen. Yerna, mačči deg usɣar n tasaft i tent-xeddmen yifellaḥen, deg yimɣan ileqqaqen am tbuda neɣ s uglim yelsan taduṭ.

# 2.2.5. Alugen n wassaɣ

Akken ad yezḍ uḍris, ilaq-as ad qqnen akk yisalan gar-asen s wassaɣ n unamek, ama deg yiwet n tefyirt, ama gar tefyar neɣ deg uḍris sumata. Ilaq ad ilin wassaɣen mwatan, banen gar tedyanin, gar tigawin d wudmawen.

# Amek ?

Deg ugni n tektiwin ara nsemmi G, ad ilin sin waddaden n tɣawsiwin K akked R mwatan ma yella K d tamentilt neɣ d turda n R.

|Md :|G d agni n tktiwin ; deg-s K, R, M :|
|---|---|
|K-|Uɣalen yifellaḥen ɣer lexla.|
|R-|Yeḥbes ugeffur.|
|M-|Ɣlayet lqahwa.|

Deg G, ad neqbel amwati ger K akked R, maca ur nesdukul ara K akked M imi ulac imezdi neɣ tasɣunt ara ten-yezdin.

# Mačči am deg :

- Ruḥen at taddart ɣer lexla acku / imi / axaṭer / yeḥbes ugeffur.

# Am deg :

- D azal. Ihi / Daymi xlan yiberdan.
- Ččḥen warrac / Ulac aman deg tala. (deg ubrid n tala i ttganin tiḥdayin).
- Ur yerbiḥ ara / yettqudur (Ma d akayad n waddal).

# Tira di tmedyazt

# Ramdane ABDENBI

Awal yettidir anda t-sseqdacen. Awal, mi ɣeflen fell-as medden ad iruḥ si tmeslayt. Asemres n wawal ajenṭaḍ ad yessenger awal anaṣli ɣas sɛan yiwen unamek di sin yid-sen. Imi tutlayt-nneɣ d timawit, idles, tigemmi d tsekla-nneɣ merra ggran-d deg wawal. Ihi ma iruḥ wawal, truḥ tilin, truḥ tɣerma d wayen icudden ɣer-s. Imira, ḥala ayen i ɣ-d-yeǧǧa wawal i nesɛa d tasekla ama deg yisefra, deg yinzan neɣ di timucuha... Si tazwara n lqern-agi iɛeddan i bdan yimnuda, yal yiwen di tallit-is, alqaḍ n wayen ara yilin imira d llsas iɣef ara nebnu azekka-nneɣ.

Ugar n wayen i d-yettwaleqḍen, yella umezruy yettwarun, maca yeḍfi taɣerma-nneɣ s tiden i d-iɛeddan di Tefriqt n Ugafa… Ihi, si tama, ma tetmeḥḥen terwiḥt, ma uzzlen idammen... ɣef tmaziɣt i wakken ad tidir, ad d-tifrir, ad tettwaru am tutlayin nniḍen, ur ilaq ara, si tama nniḍen, ad neqdec -war lebɣi neɣ war tamusni- i wakken ad tuɣal (Tamaziɣt) s anda akken tella zik : seddaw leɛnaya n timawit.

Tugget n tmedyazt taqburt i d-yettwajemɛen tettwaẓreg-d s tsuqelt s tutlayt tafransist (amedya Les Isefra de Si Mohand) neɣ s yiḍrisen i d-yessefhamen liḥala s umata, tidyanin d wayen iɣef i d-yewwi umedyaz asefru (amedya Inna-yas Ccix Muhend). TIKWAL, alamma neɣra tasuqelt neɣ aḍris ara nefhem ayen yettwarun s tmaziɣt : ad nefhem ayen i d-yenna umedyaz di tallit d temnaḍt ideg yedder imir-nni.

Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008 - 159 -
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

Imusnawen iqedcen akked widen inudan i wakken ad ḥarben ɣef tgemmi d yidles amaziɣ, ladɣa aqbayli, asmi d-jemɛen ayen ufan mi sen-tettunefk tegnit, yal yiwen deg-sen (imnuda) yura-t akken i s-yesla ɣur yimɣaren d temɣarin, ɣur yirgazen d tlawin yecfan i kra seg wayen sen-d-ǧǧan imenza-nsen di tudrin n temnaḍt n leqbayel. Isekkilen d yilugan n tira iss t-uran, d widen yellan di tallit-nni ideg ddren yimnuda-agi. Wigi d kra n yimedyaten i d-ibeggnen belli d ayen umi slan i uran akken kan ara d-yettwanṭeq s teqbaylit. Ma yettwafhem akken yella (akken yettwanṭaq) dɣa igerrez, mulac llan imerna i usefhem ama d iḍrisen ama d tasuqelt :

|Jewǧeɣ jjwaj d amessas|33|
|---|---|
|D zzwaǧ-is i-gmeḥquṛen|23|
|Yir jjwaǧ yug-it wul-iw|24|
|Ad yuɣal nek ad jewjeɣ|102|

- Kemmel awal-im 34

- Adikemmel Repp°i ussan-im di lkhir

Uran isefra akken i ten-id-yenna umedyaz, fehmen-ten akken i sen-ten-id-yessefhem. Yeggra-d i yimnuda ad ten-arun i wakken ad fehmen wiyaḍ ayen i sen-d-yessefhem umedyaz. Mi ara iɣer imeɣri tamedyazt, yessefk ad yefhem anamek yefka umedyaz i yimeslayen-is.

# Si tizi armi d t-tizi 35

Ḥed ur ten ittɛasi

S lbaṛuḍ i tt-id-ḥellan

Di taggara n usebter, Dda Lmulud yura-d :

Si Tizi Bbwekfadu ar Tizi At Ɛica.

Lemmer ur t-id-yuri ara nezmer ad nefhem ahat si Tizi n Targa ar Tizi n Wegni… ur nẓerr ara anta Tizi iɣef la d-yettmeslay umedyaz imi aṭas i yellan di tmurt n leqbayel.

# Yusa-d si Maṣeṛ

# Tunes

# Yess netwennes

Ma n-nekwni d’ aql-aɣ nuyes

Ɣas ad d-iban belli ifyar-agi ttwafhamen s sshala, maca di taggara n usebter Dda Lmulud yufa belli yessefk ad yerr tamawt :

Meḥsub : Nekwni da aql-aɣ

Tamawt-agi yerna-tt i wakken ad yessefhem i yimeɣriyen anamek n n-nekwni d’ aql-aɣ. Yettili tikwal ugar n usefhem imi imnuda ttafen belli, ahat, tira-nni iss yettwaru usefru ur ssawaḍent ara izen n umedyaz i yimeɣri ɣas nitni (imnuda) fehmen-t akken iwata lḥal. Ihi, (ma neɛreḍ ad d-nefk asteqsi-agi) acuɣer ur t-yuri ara Dda Lmulud akken yella di taggara n usebter ?

# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

# A lbaz izedɣen tignaw

Kulḥed anida s-tmal

Tikwal la nfehhem asefru si tɣuri tamezwarut. Tikwal ad t-nefhem s tsuqelt (s tefransist) i d-yesseda umnadi deg udlis. Tikwal s wayen i d-yettaru umnadi di taggara n usebter (bas de page). Ma ur nefhim ara asefru mačči ḥala tira d tunṭiqin i d ssebba imi llan daɣen imeslayen iqburen i ur nesseqdac ara imira akken llan imeslayen yemgaraden si temnaḍt ɣer tayeḍ. Ma deg wayen yerzan imeɣriyen, ma ur yettwaru ara wawal akken iwata ur t-fehhmen ara. Ma ur fhimen ara kra imeslayen ur fehhmen ara asefru.

# Mi yaɣliɣ ṭṭfeɣ sgem 40

# Tezwiḍ-iyi-d afus-iw

# Ibeddel-iyi ula d nnul

# S nnḥadi yeččuṛ-iyi

Alamma neɣra tasuqelt n usefru s tefransist ara nefhem ayen i d-yenna umedyaz i win yuran imeslayen-is :

- nnḥadi (soupirs) d nnhati.
- win ara yeɣlin ad yeṭṭef deg (di) tɣawsa mačči seg (si) :

Imi nettaru asefru akken i s-nsel, d tunṭiqin i d-yeqqar umedyaz di yal afir i nettaru ɣef lkaɣeḍ, ihi, akken i t-id-yenna umedyaz ara t-naru : ma «yezleg» wawal akken ara yeqqim, ma «iṣeggem» wawal akken ara yeqqim.

40 Tassadit Yacine, Piège, Le combat d’une femme algérienne, Essai d’anthropologie de la souffrance, Publisud/Awal, Paris, 1995, P.190-192.
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

D acu-t wawal izelgen, d acu-t win iṣeggmen? Awal «iṣeggem» di temnaḍt ahat «yezleg» di tayeḍ. Awal yura umnadi deg At Wasif mačči akken ara t-yaru umnadi nniḍen deg Uqbu. Awal qqaren-t di taddart ulac-it di tayeḍ...

Tameslayt n zik ahat ur ɣ-d-tewwiḍ ara akken iwata lḥal, kra n imeslayen ttun-ten medden, ur ten-fehhmen ara imira ma slan-asen. Taddart ideg ulac takerza amgar d ttelqim, ulac aẓeṭṭa taruka d uqerdac, ulac afexxar… d lfeṭṭa ur ttissinen ara imezdaɣ-is, ladɣa ilemẓiyen, kra n tɣawsiwin i sseqdacen di lḥirfat-agi.

D imnayen i yettmettaten

terram i utemmu

Hun-as i ddbeɣ n warkas

S tbuda bnu-d taferka-s

# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

# Ay amezraɛ n tmeclac 43

Muqel m’ ak-k-itbaɛ yimɣi Si temnaḍt ɣer tayeḍ, ad naf belli tutlayt temgarad di kra n yimeslayen yecban : ad ḍsen/ad ṭsen, yuḍen/yuṭen, remḍan/remṭan, amellal/ameyyay, leḥsab/yeḥsab… neɣ wid i d-yekkan si tutlayin nniḍen ladɣa taɛrabt imi d tutlayt n Leqran. Nettaf imeslayen yecban : ṭelbeɣ, lqelb, heǧǧaɣ, ṣṣfuf, waḥed, lqul Rrebbi, walakin, lǧawab…

# Atnaaṛeḍ a lmuṛaheb 44

aqlaɣ neddebdeb alamma iḥud uaassas D tidet, ahat, llan widen yeɣɣaren tamedyazt akken i ɣɣaren amagrad n tɣamsa ; taɣuri tamezwarut yefhem ayen yebɣa ad t-id-yini umedyaz... Llan widen umi tettɛekkir lefhama di kra n imeslayen maca ad yefhem anamek mi ara yekfu taɣuri n usefru neɣ ahat n tseddart… Llan widen umi ẓẓay unamek n usefru si tira d kra n yimeslayen ur ifehhem ara… Deg wannect-a imedyaten, ad naf belli d tunṭiqin i zemren ad cekklent anamek n usefru imi ttwarzen imeslayen seg wakken ur ttwarun ara akken iwata lḥala. Rnu i waya imeslayen yettemgaraden si temnaḍt ɣer tayeḍ, si tallit ɣer tayeḍ. Amedya n zzwaǧ (zzawaǧ s taɛrabt) yettwarun jjwaǧ, jjwaj, zzwaj, zzwaǧ ad ɣ-d-imel belli, ahat, ma yella d ameslay umi iban unamek yessefk ad yettwaru kan s yiwet tɣara ladɣa ma yella si tutlayin nniḍen i t-id-newwi. I wumi ara naru ? Amek ara naru ? Anwa i ilaq ad t-nezzwer d tunṭiqin neɣ d tira s ilugan n tjerrumt ? Akken i s-yehwu tili ccbaḥa n yimeslayen iss d-yeqqar umedyaz ayen iceɣben tallit-is, ma ur tewwiḍ ara akken i tt-yebɣa netta i widen i s-

44 Mouloud Mammeri, Les isefra de Si Mohand, Maspero, Paris, 1982, P.138, N°21.
# Tasɣunt n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa

yettḥessisen, i t-yeɣɣaren, izen-is ɣas d atrar ad t-yawi waḍu… Lemmer telli tesleḍt, ahat, ad nezzwer taɣawsa ɣef tayeḍ, maca di teswiɛt-agi tugget n yimeɣriyen d anamek iɣef la ttnadin. Ɣef waya, yewwi-d lḥal ɣef widen d-ileqqḍen ayen yellan d aqbur, imedyazen n tura yettnadin atrar, ad gerrzen tira-nsen, akken ad nefhem tamedyazt-nneɣ war tasuqelt s tutlayin nniḍen...

win ur aɣ-d-nenni ara
ur aɣ-ilzim wara
win i yaɣ-d-innan
ur nettwexxir ara
Martial Rémond, Au cœur du pays kabyle, Baconnier-Hélico, Alger, 1932.

45 Mouloud Mammeri, Inna-yas Ccix Muhend, Edité à compte d’auteur, 1990, P.153, N°227.

- 166 - Timmuzɣa Uⁿ 19 - A.U.T. / Ɣuct 2008
